![eyeDivider.gif](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.dacoinc.com%2Fimages%2FeyeDivider.gif&hash=641fe03faa648f03f7b285b9eebe78d7)


**IMPORTANT!  READ HERE FIRST: [DOX Safety Discussion Thread](https://www.bluelight.org/vb/threads/768187-The-safety-(or-lack-therof)-of-DOX-chemicals-discussion-thread)**


Original post:


I'd love to hear anything about this compound besides what can be found in PiHKAL:


"*DOSAGE: 1.5 - 3.0 mg.


DURATION: 12 - 24 h.


QUALITATIVE COMMENTS: (with 1.6 mg) I was hit with a slightly light head; the effects were quite real. I was disconnected, and somehow spacey, but this was a favorable spacey which was kind of fun. Somewhere at about the sixth hour I realized that I was beginning to drop off a bit, but six hours later yet, there was still a lot of memory. This is a long thing.


(with 2.4 mg) This is what I might call an archetypical psychedelic. Everything is there in spades, with few if any of the subtle graces, the `gentle images' and `gentle fantasies' of the 2-carbon phenethylamines. This is the works. There are visuals, and there are interpretive problems with knowing just where you really are. The place where nothing makes sense, and yet everything makes sense. I have just slept for a few hours, and now I am awake and it has been eighteen hours, and there is a lot still going on, although I have a relaxed, good feeling. Anyone who uses this had better have 24 hours at their disposal.


(with 2.4 mg) Here I am at the sixth hour, and I am still roaring along at a full plus three. I have established that this material is neither anti-erotic nor anorexic. The body is very comfortable, and so is the mind. There is an interesting aspect, perhaps peculiar only to this experiment and under these conditions. With my eyes closed the fantasy is a completely dark screen, lovely and seductive, subtle, and yet light must be deliberately brought in. This is not in any way negative for being in the dark, but is just unusual. I will have to try this in the daylight next time, to see what the eyes-closed brings to the mind-screen. At 24 hours, I have found that my sleep was not too great. My dreams were tight, and I kept defending against trouble; the nervous system was too alert. I was in a good humor, though, and I still am. This is excellent stuff, but start early in the day.


EXTENSIONS AND COMMENTARY: It is clear that the three halo-amphetamine derivatives, DOI, DOB and DOC, are all pretty much of the same potency. And all of them very long lived. The difference between the various halogen atoms was brought up under the 2C-C discussion. DOC is clearly a long-lasting, dyed-in-the-wool psychedelic. *"

<!-- POST START: id=3780201 num=4 author=fizzacyst author_id=40848 date=2005-12-20T21:48:26+0000 -->
### Post #4

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3780201 |
| Author | fizzacyst |
| Author ID | 40848 |
| Date | Dec 20, 2005 at 9:48 PM |
| Page | 1 |

After a 6mg trip, I had a lot of sore muscles.. moreso than with anything else I've taken. Some of this was probably the way I was controrting myself: crawled up on top of the dryer.. about 6 ft off the ground, 2ft from the ceiling; layed on my chest for a while, trying not to let my arms or legs touch the ground;  hanging upside down off the back of the couch; chasing the dog under a small coffee table and behind a sofa, etc..


This was on friday, and my neck felt back to normal yesterday. The strain was giving me a near constant (but tolerable) headache. Naproxen sodium fixed it.


During the trip, and for maybe 10 hours after I felt like I was having trouble with my body temperature. My head felt very hot, to the point it was uncomfortable. I asked my girlfriend to see if I felt overheated, and she didn't think so. I also checked my temperature with an "instant" thermometer (the ear kind) many many times, and it was always normal. I had to point a fan at me to get to sleep it bothered me so much. I used an oral mecury thermometer after I sobered up a bit, and it showed a normal temp as well.


It wrecked my stomach a little bit as I was coming up. It wasn't anywhere near as bad as the 2mg I took after eating french fries though. This felt more like I had too much stomach acid. I didn't have any antacids, so I tried some baking soda in water. It seemed to help a little bit, but I think it was just because it made me burp. I drank a little bit of some highly carbonated soda that did the same thing, it provided much more relief. The discomfort went away after the drug really began to take a firm hold.


A word of caution:

I really would not recommend taking more than 4mg of this stuff and going out into public unless you have tried such an amount at home first. If I had gone for a walk or to a party I wouldnt have been able to make it back. I was fried to the point that I *had* to lay down and dissolve. Maybe I'm a little more sensitive, I don't know... but its not a chance I'd want to take.

<!-- POST END: id=3780201 -->

No, it won't be that amount in each drop. And what volume of liquid are you considering to be a drop, anyway?


That scale way too inaccurate for dealing with a drug of this potency. And cold ethanol is going to be one of the more difficult substances you could choose to dissolve the stuff in. And if its near saturation (no idea what volume you mean by 150 drops), keeping it in the freezer may cause some of the drug to fall out of solution.


Loss of potency should be the absolute least of your concerns.

<!-- POST END: id=3780203 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3780204 num=11 author=fizzacyst author_id=40848 date=2005-12-21T19:05:46+0000 -->
### Post #11

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3780204 |
| Author | fizzacyst |
| Author ID | 40848 |
| Date | Dec 21, 2005 at 7:05 PM |
| Page | 1 |

Liquid measure is fine. In fact, unless you had a scale that would measure a tenth of a milligram accurately and experience dealing with very small amounts of chemicals, I wouldn't reccomend any other method.


I'm just saying that if your scale is accurate to 20mg, thats a 40mg window of error. You could think you have 100mg, but you could actually have anything between 80mg and 120mg... and thats if your scale is well made and as accurate as it is supposed to be.


So thats a range of 0.53mg to 0.8mg per drop, assuming you don't lose anything and each drop is exactly the same size (probably won't be).


So 5 drops could be a dose of 2.65mg, or 4.00mg. Thats a significant variance... and you'll never know about it until you eat it.

<!-- POST END: id=3780204 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3780328 num=13 author=Blowmonkey author_id=46604 date=2005-12-21T19:27:08+0000 -->
### Post #13

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3780328 |
| Author | Blowmonkey |
| Author ID | 46604 |
| Date | Dec 21, 2005 at 7:27 PM |
| Page | 1 |

Christ man.. DON'T USE DROPS TO MEASURE ANYTHING. Read. That scale your friend owns CANNOT measure the exact amount. It has just been explained that there will be a 40 mg margin of error, it can be 120 mg it can be 80 mg, just because you're assured it's 100  mg does NOT mean it is. 


A good solution would be 1mg per 5 ml. That's 500 ml for 100 mg. Use something like that, nothing else. If you don't listen, don't even bother asking questions anymore.


No it is not photoreactive, DOC is pretty stable, also in solution. Ofcourse you want it stored in a cool, dry, dark place to ensure there will be no loss of potency.

<!-- POST END: id=3780328 -->

Well, i tried 3mg of DOC on new years eve.


I started coming up within 30min and peaked by 75min.

While coming up i vomited once but after that i experienced no body load what so ever. In fact i enjoyed the body high.


This is definetly some really magical stuff, i could tell even from my 3mg which only got me to a weak +++. I wouldnt go comparing it to LSD though, which i consider the holy grail, but it was amazing.


During the trip i experienced no anxiety at all and had MDMA like waves of euphoria wash over me. It wasnt very visual but my mind would flow away into these deep fantasies to places i cant even really describe.


Next time i will try 5mg, as 3mg made me trip but not nearly as hard as i would have liked to. I would compare 3mg to maybe 2 hits of acid or 16mg of 2c-e in intensity.


This stuff definetly has potential, cant wait to try a higher dose.


Oh yeh, i would not recomend taking this without a benzo on hand. I was not able to fall asleep untill 19 hours after i ingested it, at which point i was very exhausted and just wanted to go to sleep but had to much energy to do so.


So, im in the camp that thinks this stuff is really amazing, just in my case i think i would need to dose higher to see its true potential.


peace,

cat

Well 10mg of DOM would be enough for me to be hard pushed to think of when I'd want to do it (ie. too much for usual settings such as festival, camping in the great outdoors etc). I think it'd have to be one of those times that you've specially set aside for one of those 'soul-searching' trips.


As such, I think that if I were to try DOC it'd be in the 1-1.5mg first time* and never greater than 3mg except for the above 10mg of DOM conditions.


***** - First 'proper dose'; as usual, I'd take a 0.1-0.2mg dose for my first ever exposure to make sure I didn't have any idiosyncratic reaction

<!-- POST START: id=3780187 num=23 author=gloggawogga author_id=40020 date=2006-01-09T02:37:15+0000 -->
### Post #23

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3780187 |
| Author | gloggawogga |
| Author ID | 40020 |
| Date | Jan 9, 2006 at 2:37 AM |
| Page | 2 |

^^^


The two times I took DOC it had a rather fast come up, with effects within the first hour and strong effects by T+2 hours. So I would say if you spread a dose out that far apart you'd get a slightly weaker but longer lasting experience then if you took it all at once.


I personally find the method of spreading out doses usefull with some psychedelics, but not others. It slows the total come up time, making it easier to settle into the experience. It also lenghthens the total duration, which may or may not be desirable. I generally like to do it with shorter lasting materials, to slow the come up and the come down. With DOC, the comedown is kinda long, and the come up wasn't too fast for me, so I wouldn't want to do it that way. But its a matter of personal preference.

<!-- POST END: id=3780187 -->

**This is getting annoying as hell...(DOC and scale questions)**


Okay, this is the 4th time I've typed out this thread, and yet, for one reason or another, this is the first time it's (hopefully) readable by others. First time it told me I'm not logged in, then I log in and everything I've typed is erased. Second time I posted it, but it got glitched and turned into a wierd "Big and Dandy DOC Thread", and of course, what I had typed was nowhere to be found. Then I typed it all out again, and once again, I tried to post and it said I wasn't logged in. I log in, and yet again, everything is erased. And I was logged in already both times. This is the shortened version of the old thread. And yeah, I know there was some kind of software problem, but I'm posting this again because I really need an answer within a few hours.


Anyway, someone I know has 2.5 mg of DOC and wants to know if he takes it at ~8:00 pm, if he'll be straight enough to seem normal (if perhaps a bit tired) by about 16-18 hours later? In other words, those of you who've tried it, about how long through the trip was it before you feel you could have at least acted "normally" around others? Include dose, tolerance, and other drugs taken if possible.


Also, if one is going to be measuring out DOC with a scale, would one accurate to 2 mg work if he used the solution method (for instance measure out 15 mg, then dissolve in 15 mL of alcohol and dose by measuring out mL's)? Seems to me like it would be fine if done that way, as inaccuracies would seem to be in the fraction of a mg range, but I'm not entirely sure (obviously it wouldn't work if one were measuring out individual doses with the scale). If it won't work, what's about the cheapest mg scale I can get that would accurately and consistently measure 1-5 mg doses?

<!-- POST START: id=3778908 num=25 author=nuke author_id=62546 date=2006-01-11T22:55:34+0000 -->
### Post #25

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3778908 |
| Author | nuke |
| Author ID | 62546 |
| Date | Jan 11, 2006 at 10:55 PM |
| Page | 2 |

The length will vary immensely depending on the chemistry of your body -- I've seen people down and out in 12 hours, and still rolling along at a +2 30 hours later (this was around 2mg with no tolerance).  Most people seem to fall between 12-24 hours, with some residue following for a while.  I wouldn't plan on appearing normal for anything in any less than 24 hours.


The best solution for weighing in this case is liquid, like you stated -- unless you're confident your scale works well to fractions of mgs (a scale with this precision will probably run you over a thousand USD).

<!-- POST END: id=3778908 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=3779013 num=26 author=bluedolphin author_id=41559 date=2006-01-11T23:39:54+0000 -->
### Post #26

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3779013 |
| Author | bluedolphin |
| Author ID | 41559 |
| Date | Jan 11, 2006 at 11:39 PM |
| Page | 2 |

I would suggest using liquid measurement for such a small amount of DOC.


If you have a scale accurate to +/- 2mg or so, you can weigh out 20mg and add that to 20ml of alcohol. Then each ml will contain 1mg of DOC once it's fully dissolved.


Even a scale accurate to 1mg will not give you an accurate enough reading if you just try to weigh out 2.5mg.


As for duration... chances are you will be able to look somewhat normal after 18 hours, but you may still be experiencing minor visuals and some body energy from the DOC at this point. It's up to you how "normal" you actually have to be. If your parents or somebody else already suspects drug use, you might want to give yourself a little more time.


Also, some people continue to "trip" for 24 hours from DOC... although 12-18 hours is more typical.

<!-- POST END: id=3779013 -->

I've taken DOC twice. Once on a full stomach and once on an empty stomach.


I highly recommend taking DOC on a full stomach, the nausea is non-existent and it does not reduce the intensity or duration of the trip at all.


I plan on taking DOC with at least some food in me from now on.

<!-- POST START: id=3785927 num=29 author=seuss1973 author_id=69669 date=2006-01-14T20:18:31+0000 -->
### Post #29

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3785927 |
| Author | seuss1973 |
| Author ID | 69669 |
| Date | Jan 14, 2006 at 8:18 PM |
| Page | 2 |

I would recomend taking it about an hour after a meal, preferably something not too heavy, like chicken teriyaki or something. Don't eat a huge meal, maybe half of what you normally would eat, and don't eat anything that is very spicy or acidic.


Also, if you're one of the folks who gets chronic nausea on psychs, apparently taking some dramamine about an hour before helps.


I haven't gotten any nausea from DOC, and I've taken it on an absolutely empty stomach and after eating a meal. 


But I have gotten some mild nausea from some other compounds. One thing that I found was if I laid down when I was coming on, and then stood up, I would get sick (maybe from the contents of my stomach moving around?) But if I went about the house doing things as I came up there was no problems.


If you feel the nausea, let yourself throw up. It's really not that bad, and you will feel a whole lot better right away.

<!-- POST END: id=3785927 -->

My first dose, i took 2mg somewhere between 30 and 45min afte eating a large amount of french fries from a fast food joint. It make me feel like I had bad acid reflux, and really bothered me for a while.


So the next time (6mg), I didn't eat for 5 hours or so before dosing. I ended up sitting by the toilet for maybe 10 minutes around the 2 hours mark. I felt like I needed to spew so bad, but I just couldn't. I slammed about 8 ounces of water and tried to gag myself. It didn't really work. I ended up vomiting like teaspoon of water, and I don't think I would have done that had I not been trying to make myself throw up and get it over with.


The nausea cleared up soon after that. Its pretty common for me to get fairly nauseous during the early part of a phenethylamine trip though

**DOC Data & Thread Summary**


OK More Data folks.  One analyzed all reports on this Bluelight thread up to 12:00 AM EST 21.1.2006 (831 total posts).  One tried to summarize all clearly reported doses of DOC (63) and include interesting errata for some possible overview data.


5.80 mg.   Overall Average Reported Dose.

4.00 mg.   Average Reported Dose if one throws out the 9 reports > 10mg.


ERRATA:


Several persons reported notable threshold activity around 250-300 micrograms (0.25-0.3 mg.).


Several persons reported very strong responses (‘fully active,’ ‘intense,’ ‘+++’) in the 1-1.5 mg. range.


At least one post alleged no effects at 4 mg.


Some reports of rectal administration.


A report of an accidental dose of 15-20 mg. rectally due to the compound being mistaken for 2C-C/2C-I.


A report of 3-6 mg. insufflated and a report of 10 mg. insufflated.


psychicpsycho reported an ingestion of 15 mg. that pretty much had him ‘done’ with psychedelics. 


blab reported notable tolerance when running up dosing as follows: 1,2,3,5,8,13,17,22mg.


crowbar reported taking doses from 0.5 mg up to 20 mg. with adverse effects being noted around 20 mg.


Nuke commented on DOB mortality in the 25-35 mg. range, possibly suggesting that all dosing should remain well below 25 mg.


Blue Dolphin noted side effects as:

“Nausea: 10%

Vomiting: 5% (half of the "nausea" group)

Body Temp Issues: 10%

"Weird Smells": 3%

Excess Stimulation: 15%

Inability to Sleep past the 20-hour mark: 35%”


gloggawogga noted some of the following reported side-effects:

“Chest pressure/pain.

Stomach pain

body temperature instability

muscle twitching/shaking

lethargy

nausea/vomiting.

seizures”


The reported doses used to calculate below:

> — Ximot said:


I smoked 0.75mg to boost my trip about 6 hours into it. I felt it almost instantly, it was only a modest boost in intensity though.


I have also smoked DOI twice. First time 1.5mg split into two doses about 30 minutes apart with a high dose of poppies, second time 2.5mg split into 2 doses about 10 minutes apart. It takes effect immediately and peaks in under five minutes. The duration is about the same as oral, maybe a little shorter. It feels quite different from an oral dose and mentally not as interesting. Visuals are just as strong though. 


The potency of DOI did not seem to be increased much if at all but if you try smoking it, be careful with the dose. It is likely that some of the chemical was destroyed by the heat, it did leave a little bit of black residue.


I don't know how potent DOC would be smoked because the only time I did it was while tripping on an oral dose and there was a lot of tolerance due to that. I may smoke a small dose when I have the time, just out of curiosity. If I try it, I will post my results in this thread.

<!-- POST START: id=3832458 num=35 author=CastorTroy author_id=76790 date=2006-02-05T00:51:08+0000 -->
### Post #35

| Field | Value |

| Page | 2 |

So, this is a kind of mini-trip report that I think is suitable to stay in this thread without me making a whole different thread for it.


I took 2mg of this stuff 9 hours ago.


Didn't feel anything for an hour. Then it just felt like a percocet for the next hour. Then for the next hour (3rd hour) it got quite intense and I had some minor visual effects. The only visuals I got lasted maybe 20 minutes and were nothing to write home about. After this experience, I realize that taking a drug to see cool things is somewhat childish. There'a a lot more you can do with your brain than see some cool fractals, guys.


From the three hour point on, it didn't feel like I was tripping at all (I've done mushrooms, salvia, and 2C-I before, so I'm not just saying that). I just felt 'turned on' to life. I was and am completely happy with everything that I am and everything that is. I read "Remember, Be Here Now" and it seemed to go with what I was thinking really well.


This didn't feel like a drug for me once 3 hour had passed. I felt almost 100% sober except for the fact that I was inredibly happy. I suppose I started 'coming down' after about 7 hours. Some effects are still persisting, but it's more or less just some kind of weird feeling in my head.


I don't know if it's because 2 mg was a low dose. But really, I feel it just kinda flicked on some kind of switch in my head and I'm changed in a way that makes me really happy with everything. It brought me to a place that I no longer need a drug to get to.


This isn't just a drug. It didn't change me. It let me change myself.

<!-- POST END: id=3832458 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3840908 num=41 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2006-02-08T19:54:36+0000 -->
### Post #41

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3840908 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Feb 8, 2006 at 7:54 PM |
| Page | 3 |

I've done DOC 3 times now, and each time I've taken it on a Friday night at 11pm, without sleeping since the morning, and been up until 11 the next night.  The first 8-12 hours of the trip are quite psychedelic, and then the plateau starts.  I usually lie down in my bed for about 2 hours during this time and just kind of trance out in half-sleep, as the drug is amazingly gentle on the body.  For me, the plateau has been quite a bit less psychedelic, and the visuals fade most of the way, and I emerge from the psychedelic haze, so to speak, into an extremely coherent, quick thinking, and humorous stage that I truly love.  I can see how some people might think they were down, since it's no longer very visual or as intense, but it's most definitely still an acute effect of the drug.


I love the two stages of DOC.  The first is deep and crazy and very memorable, and the second is a truly wonderful mood and state of mind that allows for integration of the experience and a wonderful state of mind that seems to last and last.

<!-- POST END: id=3840908 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3846834 num=44 author=CastorTroy author_id=76790 date=2006-02-11T04:44:26+0000 -->
### Post #44

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3846834 |

| Page | 3 |

So I took 5mg of DOC earlier today. Let me say that 5mg is quiiiite different than 2mg. It was pretty intense from about T+2 to T+4 hours. I had lots of strange body feelings. I got kind of sleepy for a little bit (people have been mentioning this too, and I find that SO strange!). I had that anxious PEA 'coming up' feel where it's like your mind/body is anticipating something but you dont know why or what. The bathroom tiles started swirling and climbed up the walls. That was actually the first real tripping visual I've had that did something that I knew just wasn't there. 


I don't know about you guys, but it seems to go into a different phase after about 4 hours. Almost all of the body effects go away, that strange feel of anticipation went away, and I feel a lot calmer. Just kind of high, trippy thinking, with some enhanced colors and stuff. I really like the latter phase, and it fortunately lasts a lot longer than that initial intense peak.

<!-- POST END: id=3846834 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3867746 num=45 author=Ximot author_id=50768 date=2006-02-19T12:40:44+0000 -->
### Post #45

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3867746 |
| Author | Ximot |
| Author ID | 50768 |

**Another one in the DOC-isn't-THAT-great camp**


%) After ingesting (2mg) DOC for the first time about 24 hours ago and having now woken up after 6 hours of alprazolam-induced sleep I have to say it really is far too long and a bit tiring / strenuous on the body after so many hours... I value how the compound's ability to allow me to let my emotions wash over me while at the same time to stand back and reflect quite soberly on this... also, excellent visuals at some stage, visuals definitely on par with a reasonably strong acid trip. I also appreciate the great access to acceptance and wisdom the compound seems to offer. It allowed me to be creative, but it really, really, really does get groggying after so many hours... it is metabolised a little slowly, and for me it wasn't entirely without body issues (high body temperature, bloated red face with blotchy skin at the T+12hour mark following the insufflation of a mere 30mg of K and the ingestion of 1mg 5-MeO-DIPt and 3mg MIPT <-- don't even ask why I did this!! I really can't even begin to explain) ...  after benzo induced sleep and some coral mineral and activated charcoal and sea salt intake as well as heaps of liquids my face now looks quite normal again though and I probably don't look worse than anyone who had a few beers too many the night before though ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)


I could imagine taking this compound again, probably at a higher dose (6mg??) in order to experience the much-touted "vortex reality" but I feel that this maybe at least a year or so in the future. The diifficult metabolisation that psychedelic amphetamines (I had some body issues with DOI, too) seem to have for my body even at 2mg and the ensuing extremely long duration really make this something I will be mostly staying away from in the future.

<!-- POST END: id=3867746 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3869870 num=47 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2006-02-20T14:22:42+0000 -->
### Post #47

| Field | Value |

Hmm... I haven't even ever come close to puking on DOC, and I have it in a water and alcohol suspension and absorb it mostly sublingually, all at once.  It just seems to come on slowly enough that it never bothers my stomach at all.


An another note, that 4mg experience I mentioned the other day was really intense and very different from my other experiences.  I'll be writing a report soon.  I didn't reach this "vortex reality", but the entire experience (friday and saturday) felt totally unreal.  I experienced time in very strange ways - it was 2:47 for about half the night it seems, then it was 6:30, then it was 4:50, etc, etc... I tried reading some ketamine trip reports on Erowid because at lower dosages I've found it to greatly enhance my ability to "get into" a written report or other piece of literature and feel like the experience has happened to me, but I just had the same one up from 2am to 6:30 or 8:40, whichever it was when I went to bed.  I just kept reading tiny sections of it and then getting stuck into some massive train of thought.  Strangely, there wasn't anything I'd call a body "load", but the intense energy running through my body was making me constantly squirm about, in a pleasant but very insistent way.  I went to bed at some point as it was getting light, and I don't remember falling asleep, just closing my eyes and then opening them, afetr existing in a field of color.  I honestly felt a little possessed or something ther whole time, like my body was being occupied by myself and something else and I only had partial control.


Very weird.  This was certainly more memorable (though disjointed) than my lower dosages, but VERY different.


Oh, and I really love the length of DOC.  The other very long-lasting drugs like 5-MeO-AMT (ick) that I've tried have lasted annoyingly long, but I just love the next day with DOC, where you're into the second leg of the journey.  it makes for a fun Saturday where I'm in a great and curious and joyful mood with an awesome body buzz.  I also react much better to small amounts of alcohol on that day after, as generally even small amounts of alcohol make me feel kind of poisoned and gross.

<!-- POST END: id=3869870 -->

### Post #56

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3886055 |
| Author | illuminati boy |
| Author ID | 70954 |
| Date | Feb 27, 2006 at 12:08 AM |
| Page | 3 |

**DOC Usage Frequency Data**


Some preliminary data from a survey on DOC indicates that:


40.9 % reported using DOC 1 time

36.4 % reported using DOC 2-5 times

  9.1 % reported using DOC 5-10 times

13.6 % reported using DOC 10-20 times


2 respondents skipped this question


These numbers are from an anonymous survey so they may be skewed, though it is likely that they are fairly reliable (no really big outliers so far).  If anything they may slightly underrepresent the number of uses as some respondents may have used DOC additional times since the survey was completed.  In general though, the data points to most persons (77.3 % ) having used DOC 1-5 times in total.


I B

<!-- POST START: id=3891615 num=58 author=trypt author_id=55775 date=2006-03-01T03:38:23+0000 -->
### Post #58

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3891615 |
| Author | trypt |
| Author ID | 55775 |
| Date | Mar 1, 2006 at 3:38 AM |
| Page | 3 |

Has anyone tried sublingual DOC successfully?  I tried 1mg DOC sublingually two weeks ago, got little effects, barely threshold, got very minor CEVs after smoking cannabis.  Didn't notice much else in terms of the DOC, except a very minor "presence" that something more than cannabis was effecting me.  This presence went away after about 6-7 hours.  


Last week I tried a 1.25mg sublingual dose.  I got low, but noticeable effects out of the DOC.  After smoking cannabis, I got distinct CEVs, but nothing to write home about.  My open-eye vision seemed 'sharper.'  Also, I could feel a psychedelic mindstate creeping up, but never quite took hold.  I more or less just got a little "confused."  Laughing seemed to come more easily.  Duration was about 6-8 hours again.


My main question is regarding the method of absorption.  My first trial was by swiping up 1mg of DOC from a glass plate with my finger, and wiping my finger off (and hopefully the DOC) under my tongue.  After not swallowing any saliva for about 45 minutes, I spit all the saliva out of my mouth.  Do you think this was efficient?  Specifically, was 45 minutes enough time for the DOC to absorb?


My second trial was with improvised blotter paper (140lb. watercolor paper).  I ended up having to use EIGHT square inch pieces of paper to absorb all of the alcohol/DOC solution.  I kept these eight pieces of paper under my tongue for about 30 minutes, then sort of mashed them up with my teeth, but still kept them in my mouth, for another half hour.  After having the paper in my mouth for 60 minutes, and not swallowing any saliva, I spit everything out.


Is 45-60 minutes enough time for the DOC to absorb sublingually (considering it's supsended in blotter paper)?  Also, how do you suggest I concentrate my DOC/alcohol solution so, for instance, .25ml = 1mg as opposed to 1ml = 1mg?  I was thinking I could just drop out the dose I want onto a piece of aluminum foil, let most of the alcohol evap, then dip the blotter in the (smaller) pool of alcohol. But, as the alcohol evaporates, won't it leave behind some DOC clinging to the walls of the aluminum foil?


Any ideas would be appreciated.

<!-- POST END: id=3891615 -->

| Page | 3 |

I've always taken DOC sublingually because for some reason I always end up dosing it shortly after eating.  I have it dissolved in a solution containing probably 35% ethanol and the rest distilled water, and I hold it under my tongue for about 15 minutes and swallow.  It starts at about 45 minutes to an hour, and hits fully around 2 to 2.5 hours in, with a peak at maybe 4 hours.


I very much doubt it's any different from oral consumption, unless you're trying to avoid having it slowed down by the contents of your stomach.

<!-- POST END: id=3892651 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3896310 num=60 author=folias author_id=78837 date=2006-03-02T23:56:49+0000 -->
### Post #60

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3896310 |
| Author | folias |
| Author ID | 78837 |
| Date | Mar 2, 2006 at 11:56 PM |
| Page | 3 |

I've taken DOC at 2.7mg, 4.4mg and 7mg, a couple of weeks spaced apart. 


The first time I took it @ 2.7mg I think I was surprised at how deep it took me into a field of Gaiain connectivity... with full power earth/human activation which was archetyptally yogic in its imagery and energy. 


I also found I was also to go deep into releasing limitations based on conceptions or images I had made of life before I was five years old... very strong releases here...


I found I was able to let go and come into a sense of stillness and transparency which enabled my energy body to move and free itself from the chains of emotional denial... 


At this dose the +3 effects would have only lasted a few hours... I dosed at 6.30am and was able to sleep fine that night with a little valium. 


When I took it @ 4.4mg, it was not signifcantly stronger, I felt like I sincerely cracked something open with the first dose and this dose was consolidating that. 


Most of the time, I let my jaw go, and shake and just release fear... I could see a visual/organic field, but I was separate from it... kind of like mushrooms, very orange and brown. 


It was a very pleasant contemplative day....no major revelations. 


On that day, I took it at 8.30am and got to sleep @ 2am. 


A couple of week later, I took 7mg to see what would happen if I went "in there" for a number of hours...  having no idea what to expect really. I took it at 3pm. 


This was an unexpectably strong dose.... it was truly psychedelic in the way that 1000 mics of clean acid is. 


The messages and imprints and visuals coming through were very different though, they had their own texture and particular perspective... I was able to go about as deep into my own somatic and emotional, genetic imprints as I have ever gone... allowing much realisation and seeing. 


I am someone who has been working intensively with ayahuasca for 6 years or so... so it was surprising to me that I was able to go this far with this material!


(ayahuasca tends to be quite cosmic for me!) 


Now, the other thing is that it took about two weeks to feel fully physically repaired from this experience... it was definately communicated to me that this compound could very well be deleterious at high doses. 


And so I couldn't recommend a dose as high as 7mg whatsoever! 


I also couldn't recommend DOC as an LSD replacement... as a 'tripping' tool... it is just too serious and hardcore... it cuts very deep and yet has something of a throwaway disposable cartoonish element to it.... the compound came to once and pronounced its full chemical name in a radiohead ok computer voice, and said, "they call me the christ maker!" and I had this image of "DOC" as a "Bender" like figure operating on "the average age of the combat psychonaught - 19", on a stretcher... perhaps a bit too Dr Nickish for my liking! 


I also heard yells and should and squeels of urban violence and gang warfare and of kids challenging each other to take more and more DOC. 


I also felt there were beings using this compound to take readings and survaille humanity. 


I didn't feel comfortable with the morphic fabric of this material, seemingly being relatively young Nth Americans... a very slanted perspective of the world... 


(their skin screases are becoming darkier and dorkier!) 


After the profusion of personal information and processing, I blacked out,  screaming and convulsing for a few hours... I don't remember most of this... so I am told. 


I am used to this kind of thing at high doses of any psychedelic... and it doesn't concern me, if I am coming into contact with my own pain or there is some kind of struggle or movement there, I feel this is something positive. 


I "came to" at about 3am...feeling surprisingly positive...much had been revealed certainly! 


There is real power in this material.  It cuts deep... at one point, I was watching the setting sun and felt the energy move through my body and spiral through my body, feeling very penetrated by it all...  


I took DOB six years and it changed my life, in the way it allowed me to connect and work with various levels of psychic and earth energies... 


I feel the value in these series of compounds lies in connecting with the earth and consciously choosing to work through, particulary deep emotional material blocking ones growth and progress. 


The text book for DOC I would suggest is Chogyam Trungpa's "The Myth of Freedom"


[http://www.translatum.gr/buddhism/trungpa-chogyam.htm](http://www.translatum.gr/buddhism/trungpa-chogyam.htm)


A quote from this book: 


"The purpose of a true spiritual friend is to insult you!"  


Julian.

<!-- POST END: id=3896310 -->

Also, man, the DOC visuals are something else.  I get some sort of "magic eye" effect with them sometimes, too.  I'll see, for example, shining bars of light when I look at the bathtub, but they appear to be floating somewhere in the space between it and me.

<!-- POST START: id=3910494 num=63 author=specialspack author_id=19902 date=2006-03-07T16:28:35+0000 -->
### Post #63

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3910494 |
| Author | specialspack |
| Author ID | 19902 |
| Date | Mar 7, 2006 at 4:28 PM |
| Page | 4 |

So far, my only experience with DOC was low, 1.6mg (+/- 5%). 


I was suprised at the brevity of the peak effects, given the long overall duration - the peak visual and mental changes were present for at most 3 hours, then tailing off quite quickly after that.


I found it very lethargic in therapeutic terms - any attempts to do serious cognititve delving was met with a kind of "ah I just can't really be bothered" by both body and mind. This may have been to do with the unpleasent background GI disturbances which were present throughout the experience, which tinged my thought processes negatively.


However, at t+11 hrs, I insufflated ~200mg ketamine, and had a very pleasent experience - the imagery was multilayered and complex as always, but included anrogeny, guitar feedback, and deserts (no doubt helped by listening to Earth Phase 3: Thrones and Dominions - specifically "Agni Detonating over the Thar Desert").


After recovering from that, I was treated to some helpful insights towards my own attitude to mortality, and felt suggested that this would be a good subject to explore again, as well as some timely re-framing of some of my harder to live with personal attitudes.


These insights were not particulary deep, but very welcome, and helpful pointers to further areas of exploration.

<!-- POST END: id=3910494 -->

I guess anything on the 4 position that keeps it from being eaten by MAO and won't degrade into psilocin would be stuff i'd wanna try out ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png).

<!-- POST START: id=3918889 num=71 author=Ximot author_id=50768 date=2006-03-10T20:47:16+0000 -->
### Post #71

| Field | Value |

Dunno how people can do DOx compounds so often. They are so long-lasting that, for me anyway, it is out of teh question to do them regularly - even on a monthly basis would feel way too often for me. I find them more stressful than 2Cs and even most tryptamines. And I can imagine there's a huge tolerance with it. If it takes the body that long to metabolise the stuff, it is not surprising that tolerance will remain for quite some time afterwards. Up to 2 weeks, maybe more even?? Even with 2Cs done weekly I found that some minimal tolerance issue remains.


Seems to me DOC and the liek are not made to be ingested so often... tolerance being one reason, the long duration and body stress factor (that some have reported on) being another.


But maybe I'm just too old physically and mentally to want to ingest something that strong too often. ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

<!-- POST END: id=3918889 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3919038 num=72 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2006-03-10T21:54:37+0000 -->
### Post #72

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3919038 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 10, 2006 at 9:54 PM |
| Page | 4 |

When I first got my DOC, I did it 3 weekends in a row, each time on Friday night.  I noticed a VERY slight tolerance, but each dose (2mg, 3mg, then 4mg) was substantially stronger than the last.  The thing that was reduced, however, was the later stage of clarity and comprehension.  With my first 2mg dose, it was tremendous, and I felt like my mind had been clarified to a shocking extent.  it was truly awesome.  The next time the peak was more intense, but the later phase was less euphoric, and the third time, (with 4mg) the peak was so intense I can hardly remember parts of it, but the later phase was almost nothing like it was with the first experience.  it was still enjoyable but didn't have that "sparkle" of the first experience.

<!-- POST END: id=3919038 -->

<!-- POST START: id=3956188 num=73 author=gloggawogga author_id=40020 date=2006-03-26T20:19:33+0100 -->
### Post #73

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3956188 |
| Author | gloggawogga |
| Author ID | 40020 |
| Date | Mar 26, 2006 at 8:19 PM |
| Page | 4 |

I used DOC for a third time a couple of weeks ago. I dosed 5.5 mg at 7:00 PM and, not even expecting to, dosed off at about 6:30 am till about 8:30 am. I had just layed in bed in a rather content state, still somewhat awe inspired, not really expecting to get any sleep, but just resting my body. The two hours of sound sleep was a pleasant surprise. I wasn't planning on being productive in the following day after the trip, but for me two hours sleep vs. no sleep at all is the difference between feeling a little off and feeling like shit.


This was quite a contrast from my first DOC trip, where I found the effects speedy and uncomfortable. I think it just shows you the power of the mind over the body. During the first trip the dose was too low to impress me with psychedelic effects, and so I dwelled on the uncomfortable sensations in my body, only making them worse.


I spent most of the peak of the trip going for a walk in the park, it was a mild clear night. I got lost in thinking about numerous thought experiments in physics, in particular information theoretic approaches to developing QM as a principle theory. This is a problem some theoretical physicists have been working on the last 15 years or so, mainly due to the advent of quantum computing, which I've been studying over the last few months. While I certainly didn't come up with any great revelations, I found this drug profoundly useful for these types of contemplations in physics. 


For example, for split moment contemplating the gravity/acceleration postulate that underlies general relativity, the nature of hyperbolic geometry (curved space time) became as immediately intuitive to me as euclidean geometry normally is. In fact, I had never visualized hyperbolic geometry so clearly. However, this is certainly not a drug to grab a pencil and piece of paper and start writing out math or physics equations. I could 'see' hyperbolic geometry with clarity but no way could I do proofs in it, just like one can typically 'see' euclidean geometry but doing actual proofs in it is another issue. Still, it was great just to 'see' it like I had never seen it before.


The clarity of and depth insight on this drug is amazing. I suspect this drug can be a good tool for almost any deep contemplation you wish to have. But preserving that clarity while translating such insights into sober terminology is another challenge entirely.

<!-- POST END: id=3956188 -->

I have been looking over the [data I have received so far on DOC,](http://www.surveymonkey.com/DisplaySummary.asp?SID=1745359&U=174535967586) and it looks interesting.  Assuming there is not some sort of super-hype placebo effect or large response bias driving the data, this really is a very powerful psychedelic compound.  The PiHKAL entry where someone talked about “This is what I might call an archetypical psychedelic. Everything is there in spades…” seems to have hit the nail on the head.  Then again, I just read on another board a post by TokeTrip about how some teenagers under 18 all went to the hospital on account of taking massive (and possibly “eyeballed”) doses of DOC.  They reportedly took 8 mg., 15 mg., & 25 mg.!  This one is starting to sound like its DOM cousin… potentially of great use to some and soon to become the bane of ER staff (much to the joy of the DEA, Dr. Phil, Oprah, & co.).  If this should start regularly showing up on blotter… ugh…


I B


PS (Reportedly at least one of the admitted persons was tested for drugs, but did not test + for anything)

While 2,0mg of DOC produced only the slightest treshold effects, 2,5mgs produced very noticeable effects that were clearly pronounced with cannabis.


There was very little bodyload, the comeup was smooth and no anxiety at all. A relaxed and a pretty euphoric mind state, very little confusion. There was some muscle tension in the muscles of the back and neck but it didn't get too uncomfortable. No real visuals, although with eyes closed there would have been. I was in a public place so I was reluctant to keep my eyes closed for long enough to get into the visuals.


I'm unsure how steep the dosage curve after the 2,5mg point will be, I suspect 3,0mgs will produce open eye visuals and produce more confusion.


I'm also suprised that I can sleep around 6-7 hours after the comeup.

Is the insomnia closely related to the dose? What are your experiences?

<!-- POST START: id=3959062 num=76 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2006-03-27T20:58:58+0100 -->
### Post #76

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 3959062 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 27, 2006 at 8:58 PM |
| Page | 4 |

The dosage seems to vary between people.  For me, 2mg of DOC produced very few visuals but a definitely strong mental change.  2.5mg produced definite distinctive visuals and a slightly chaotic headspace.  3.2mg produced a massively strong, somewhat delerious state which I just posted a report about, with amazingly intense visuals and a peeling back of reality coupled with receptiveness to a collective reptilian consciousness.  From my experience, I'd say the dose response curve is quite steep.  On the other hand, some people on these boards take 10-12mg and get weaker effects than I've reported from 3.2.  So it seems quite variable.  Then again, I have the feeling that some people constantly exaggerate their doses, or take psychedelic every day and have a massive tolerance.


I too can sleep on DOC.  It's really a very gentle psychedelic for how intense it is.

<!-- POST END: id=3959062 -->

**Unfortunate Updates**


Recently a number of unfortunate incidents have come to my attention involving DOC.  The first is a [published newspaper report](http://www.hometownlife.com/apps/pbcs.dll/article?AID=/20060601/NEWS22/606010659/1039/RSS15)of several teenagers being hospitalized due to psychological abreactions.  The second is a report of a death involving someone who was driving under the influence of DOC.


Excerpt from an article originally published June 1, 2006 in Michigan USA:


> New drug leads to teen's overdose
> 
> 
> 
> … Troy officers investigated an incident involving a drug called "DOC."
> 
> 
> 
> It began May 24, when Bloomfield Township police officers reported a 17-year-old girl from their town was taken to the hospital for a possible drug overdose. She reportedly had been at a house on Malvern in Troy where she claimed she took the drugs. Officers responded to the home, where the 19-year-old man who lived at the home refused them entry. 
> 
> 
> 
> While speaking with the 19-year-old, officers learned three other individuals within the home were experiencing reactions to the same substance. An 18-year-old man from Bloomfield Hills was seen walking into the walls, dazed and completely naked. He was brought to the door and taken to the hospital. Two other men from Bloomfield Township, 18 and 19 respectively, that also reportedly ingested the substance, were disoriented and dazed. They also were brought out and taken to the hospital. 
> 
> 
> 
> The three men were evaluated and later released.
> 
> 
> 
> … Investigation revealed he purchased a drug called "DOC" in crystalline form, and based on information he obtained from a Web site, mixed it into a liquid and soaked art paper with the solution. He cut it into pieces and was selling and giving it away at the party.
> 		
> Click to expand...


More discussion and the complete article can be found [HERE](http://www.bluelight.ru/vb/showthread.php?t=256509).


Originally posted on another Forum.  Quoted in entirety as posted by tc_omega:

DOC gave me a whole new life perspective. But also has ruined me. My friend died while driving under the influence on it, while I was in the car. They never found it in his system though. So is it like lsd? That it just goes to your spine? 
>

> 		
> Click to expand...


I am attempting to confirm the veracity of this report, including the actual date, location, etc.


It looks like DOC is both increasingly available and increasingly being used by people with little detailed knowledge or responsibility.  I have said it before, but it probably bears repeating: This one may well have “the glory and the doom sealed up in it” like its methyl cousin.

I've read through some of this thread, some of the info on Erowid, even looked itup in PihKAL or TihKaL. But I still don't know enough about it yet to decide whether it's worth trying... So I h ave some questions. 

1)  Is DOC the kind of psychedelic that can offer deep psychological insights?

2)  Is it fun just to explore the DOC experience?  Does it offer good visuals?  Does it enhance creativity and the imagination?  Does it enhance the ability to visualize or mentally image something from imagination or memory? enhance Kundalini yoga practice?

3)  From reading Shulgin's brief report on it, I've learned that 1.5 - 3.0 or so mg DOC lasts about 20 hours.  That's a long time to set aside.  So if I were to take it but got bored with the trip after 4 or 5 hours, would I be able to sleep? to read a book? go mountain biking? or to work on that computer science project, for example?

<!-- POST START: id=4171097 num=80 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2006-06-19T21:48:51+0100 -->
### Post #80

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4171097 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Jun 19, 2006 at 9:48 PM |
| Page | 4 |

In response to your questions, socko:


1) Yes, it is for sure.  However, personally I've found it to be a "noisy" psychedelic, in that it provides you with so much visual and aural stimulation that it makes it difficult to concentrate.  It also contains quite a bit of mind fuck at 3.5-4mg, which is also where it starts to get profound.  The result is that I've not yet determined how to really let myself go during the experience after about 5 or 6 trips with it.  I've often ended up getting stuck in a loop of doing the same things over and over again, stuck on the same minute of the clock for seemingly the majority of the peak.  But DOC is really, really powerful, and I think it allows you to connect with your subconscious/unconscious mind very easily if you can work out how, which is the same as the universal consciousness.  it doesn't seem to deal with personal issues much like I find the 2Cs to do.  At least this has been my experience. 


2) Yes, the state is quite fun to explore.  it's shockingly intense, while remaining pretty emotionally steady and non-scary.  I've had great trips that ended up being primarily recreational, just because the body high feels pretty good, not too stimulating (though definitely stimulating), and the visual effects are tremendous.  Also keep in mind that, for me, it took until the 4th trial to really fully be able to enter the state.  That trial was with 4mg and was the first really hard trip I had on it.  From then on, each new trip has picked up where the last one left off, and it's gotten more and more intense and serious and deep each time.  Also, it only takes me 3mg now to get to at least the same level that the 4mg trip got me to.


3) Definitely, absolutely not at 4 or 5 hours!  it builds pretty quickly, and I'm usually starting to peak by 2 hours or just after, but the peak reaches a peak at about 5-6 hours at which point I'm fairly incapacitated, and frankly unable to be bored, due to the intense psychedelic stimulation and mindfuck.  After about 8 hours I can sometimes fall into a sleeplike trance which definitely isn't full sleep (as I usually take it at around 11 at night), and then the whole next day I'm lightly tripping.  I go back down to a +2 at about T+8 to 10, and ride that out until about T+16, and then I'll be at a +1 again until I actually sleep, no matter how long that is (it's been up to T+30 after ingestion).  I personally really, really enjoy this day after light trip though, although some people find it annoying.  Once I reach a +2 I could go out and do stuff, but there's a fair amount of pupil dilation and paranoia when in public.  During the day, the visuals from DOC while outside are miraculous and truly beautiful beyond words.  I've driven at T+10 before but I don't recommend it, although I ended up driving for about 3 hours into the mountains.


DOC is one of my all-time favorite psychedelics, but in my opinion it's difficult to use constructively, and in fact I've not yet figured out exactly how to do so.  Although I have made progress.  You can search for my posted experiences in Trip Reports if you want, as I think they illustrate the experience that I have on it pretty well.

<!-- POST END: id=4171097 -->

"IT" is all an illusion set up to teach me how to come merge with the program, learn how to go with the flow like everything else (permanent ego/self death eventually) and purely rely in intuition alone.

| Post ID | 4179206 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |

| Page | 5 |

It's legal, although it could be prosecuted under the Analogue Act since it's so similar to DOB and DOM.  But I've never heard of anyone being prosecuted for any of the "RCs" except for selling them.  In any case, even if it's not expressly illegal, no one in authority would look kindly on it.  And at the rate things are going... illegality is inevitable, I fear.  Just like with everything else.  I sometimes feel bad about talking about these psychedelics here online, because all it really does is spread the word.  But then again, the value of free and unbiased knowledge may just make it worth it.

<!-- POST START: id=4327658 num=93 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2006-08-21T04:35:01+0100 -->
### Post #93

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4327658 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Aug 21, 2006 at 4:35 AM |
| Page | 5 |

Have you tried low doses, like 1-1.5mg?  It reminds me of all-day-long MDMA with a much clearer head and an intense analytical edge, less "force", more energy, more control, and not at ALL pushy (due to the length).  At higher doses it really is nearly impossible to communicate or sometimes even think much at higher doses.

<!-- POST END: id=4327658 -->

<!-- POST START: id=4471591 num=102 author=subdefy author_id=53603 date=2006-10-16T23:14:13+0100 -->
### Post #102

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4471591 |
| Author | subdefy |
| Author ID | 53603 |
| Date | Oct 16, 2006 at 11:14 PM |
| Page | 6 |

I finally got around to trying this gem. I dosed 8mg in the form of blotters as my inital dose to start off one of my first (and subsequently last) experience at a psytrance festival. During the comeup there was some initial nausea which required me to set aside the san pedro ground cactii I was gelcapping in order to not become overwhelmed from the smell (this is quite common while coming up from anything for me). I find water usually from the tap to be alleviating to this nausea. 


The trip was actually very mild for me, I got all of the usual positive amphetamine-like effects with very little negative effects. I believe the only one I recall was while coming down my jaw was slightly moving uncontrollably but I never felt as if I was in any danger despite absolutely hating the music. The festival didn't turn out well mostly because it's not my "scene", I rather have music compliment rather than dominant whatever I am doing. The 8mg lasted from approximately 12 hours with a very smooth come down.


Despite it being very mild, it taught alot of valuable lessons that I have slowly begun to incorporate into my life. This is probably attributed to the setting and interacting with almost everyone I could run into. Someone on here described this effect as a sort of "social butterfly" which would sum it up quite well. There also seemed to be a period for about a week after the trip that I was not myself. I suppose there was a period of a week of integration for me personally.

<!-- POST END: id=4471591 -->

<!-- POST START: id=4471661 num=103 author=Ximot author_id=50768 date=2006-10-16T23:38:42+0100 -->
### Post #103

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4471661 |
| Author | Ximot |
| Author ID | 50768 |
| Date | Oct 16, 2006 at 11:38 PM |
| Page | 6 |

I wonder if I might enjoy DOC more in a well and truly social (read: party/going out) setting than completely alone or with just one person. But I doubt such a high dose would be appropriate for me. I tripped balls on 2mg and would probably take 0.5mg for such an undertaking. 


Seems DOC really has different strength for different people... while some trip hard on 2mg, others can take over 8mg and find it mild. I am pretty sensitive to all psychedelics unless I have some tolerance, but I can go pretty high on 4-substituted tryptamines and some 2C's without feeling too uncomfortable. With DOC I don't even want to find out what a high dose would do to me. I'd be too afraid that the body issues I had when on it weren't psychosomatic (set related).

<!-- POST END: id=4471661 -->

<!-- POST START: id=4472671 num=105 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2006-10-17T18:17:05+0100 -->
### Post #105

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4472671 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Oct 17, 2006 at 6:17 PM |
| Page | 6 |

DOC is odd in its dose-reponse curve.  That curve varies for me with seemingly no consistency at all.  For example, this past Saturday morning I took 1.2mg and had an incredibly visual experience, consisting of long, detailed, fractallized tracers and a visual soup effect, as well as incredible color saturation, but with relatively little mental effects.  The highest I've taken it was 5mg, but that trip didn't approach the intensity of my 3.5mg trip which was my best one of all, loaded with ego-dissolving mental effects.  The one thing DOC always seems to give me is a powerful visual experience.  I've only had a few trips on anything that were more visual than my average DOC experience, and those were my two significant 2C-E trips, which were about equal but different, and n,n-DMT.  When I take it sparingly, with long breaks in between, it feels extremely emotionally and spiritually healing, and produces a state of complete contentment with living in the now for the next 36 or so hours.  It motivates me to be a better person, more honest with myself, and more motivated.  It brings about a massive joy that rivals MDMA except which is much less forced and much more real.  I sometimes get unpleasant amphetamine side effects, and sometimes I get none of those.  It seems rather random.  DOC also shifts my mind into a very piercing analytical state, where I just want to talk and talk and talk and analyze everything I see.  It makes it seem as if everything I do, whether it's important or as useless as watching crap TV, is very useful to my understanding of the world we live in.  This state usually emerges after the peak ends.  During the peak I'm generally rather overwhelmed and it's sometimes difficult to communicate.


Overall, it's still one of my absolute favorites.  I also find that taking it the morning after an LSD trip produces a more profound state.  I think sometime soon I'm going to try mixing it with something else after the peak ends.  Maybe smoke some DMT on it.  I also have a feeling that 2C-B would mix very well.


Another thing I've noticed is that the amphetamine body issues do not seem to significantly increase with a higher dosage, at least up to the level I've taken it to (5mg).  I get the same issues from 1mg as I do from 5, if I get them at all.

<!-- POST END: id=4472671 -->

<!-- POST START: id=4473998 num=110 author=e1evene1even author_id=81284 date=2006-10-18T05:15:44+0100 -->
### Post #110

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4473998 |
| Author | e1evene1even |
| Author ID | 81284 |
| Date | Oct 18, 2006 at 5:15 AM |
| Page | 6 |

I can't wait to try this one. Its been top of my list for months now. I guess the duration can really be a downside when you don't have much time for tripping. I have never tried any DOx compounds but I do remember LSD always overstaying its welcome when I just wanted to sleep. 


This seems to be one of the most common complaints with DOC (i.e its hard to sleep for a very long time after the trip wears off). I would think that a benzo would make sleep possible around hour 12-14  or so, although I wouldn't want to think what could happen during a DOC/benzo blackout. 


I don't have very much experience with benzos but 0.5mg of Xanax knocked me out amazingly after a recent 2C-I  experience. I was a bit tired in the morning but I feel like I slept VERY well. I find melatonin (which is normally great as a sleep aid) does not work at all on psychedelic comedowns. Perhaps this is because the same receptors are involved (melatonin being a tryptamine of course) and there is competition at the receptor site, or even some kind of cross-tolerance between tryptamines (although I would find this somewhat strange with melatonin)

<!-- POST END: id=4473998 -->

I found with DOC, it was possible to fall into a trance-like "sleep?" between 8 and 14 hours after eating the stuff. Actually on my largest dose (4-5mg) I fell asleep the soonest. Honestly I'm not sure if it was real sleep or some kind of dissociation, but I was tired as hell when I fell into it and felt very refreshed and ready for the next day when I snapped back to consciousness. Still tripping mildly too ... but just enough to make the day a little sparkly.


Xorkoth what effects do you experience around 1mg? I assume this is sub-psychedelic (or I should say, sub-visual?)... 


To me, the body-load does not get any worse between 2mg and 5mg.... it remains remarkably smooth. So that would not be a motivation for me to dose low... the motivation would be, I suppose, if it sounded worthwhile.


I have no plans to eat DOC ever again but I don't always go by my plans ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

### Post #115

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4475024 |
| Author | Xorkoth |

Actually, at 1mg I often experience visuals, but not always.  It seems random.  This past Saturday I actually took 1.2mg and had very strong visuals, including morphing, particles appearing out of the air, and extreme fractallized trails.  It was actually quite shockingly and unexpectedly visual.  As for mental effects, it enhances my mood significantly and puts my mind into a highly analytical state, and makes me able to effortlessly live in the moment.


I also am able to "sleep" (more like trancing out) on DOC at any dose I've tried, after the peak ends.  I've even taken it at midnight and fallen into a trance by 6am.  Anytime I do this (take it at night), the entire next day is spent with a psychedelic amphetamine plateau/afterglow, which really makes the day fun and great and interesting.

<!-- POST START: id=4834083 num=123 author=e1evene1even author_id=81284 date=2007-03-13T21:37:23+0000 -->
### Post #123

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4834083 |
| Author | e1evene1even |
| Author ID | 81284 |
| Date | Mar 13, 2007 at 9:37 PM |
| Page | 7 |

**Finally!**


SO I finally managed to get some of this stuff. It seems to be perfect timing as well. My work schedule has changed from 6 days a week to 3 days on, 4 days off (yes I know, how lucky). I also have an ample supply of benzos (k-pin, xanax, valium), just in case things were to get out of hand and also some Risperdal M-Tabs, which are the ultimate safety net should some type of major crisis or emergency occur. I don't plan on using these things, its mostly for the piece of mind that I could.


I have around 30mg of DOC, which I plan to weigh multiple times on my American Weigh (JP Precision) milligram scale (not the best) and then dissolve in 60ml of vodka. Which means 0.5mg/ml and with a 1ml graduated pipette, I should be able to dose fairly accurately. I just went to the chemistry store and got some amber glass vials, a few 30ml measuring cups and some 1ml pipettes. I believe this should be everything I need (I've never done any serious liquid measurements before). Is vodka a good choice for DOC (and store in the freezer), or is there any advantage to distilled water?


I've never done a DOx compound before so I plan on starting low, 2mg max. I am only 135lbs so that should be a good starting point, maybe even 1.5mg. I don't want to get sucked into any vortexes just yet, but at the same time I don't want to be underwhelmed.  I'm looking forward to a long trip, for some reason my trips always end up being short these days (I usually trip 3-4 times per month). 2C-B lasts 3-4 hours, 4-AcO-DMT 2-3 hours, and LSD 6 hours. 


I am extremely intrigued about the enhanced musical abilities people have been talking about. Music is my life, if I could actually write/record songs in the later stages of a DOC trip, it would be a blessing. 


I'll also be able to take some EEG and EKG measurements (for entertainment purposes only of course). I'm particularly interested in DOC's effects on frontal lobe gamma amplitude/coherence and also Internal Cardiac Coherence/HRV. Frontal lobe gamma amplitude/coherence has recently been shown to be a correlate of 'higher states of consciousness' (in studies involving Tibetan monks) and I don't really think this has been looked at before in psychedelic studies. Should be fun nonetheless.

<!-- POST END: id=4834083 -->

<!-- POST START: id=4836478 num=126 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2007-03-14T18:00:38+0000 -->
### Post #126

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4836478 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 14, 2007 at 6:00 PM |
| Page | 7 |

eleveneleven:


I think 2mg is a good starting dose.  Have you taken any DOX substance before?  DOC is similar in character to the others, but gentler than DOB/DOI at least.  It's rather sedating, to me honest, and quite laid back, even when it becomes intense.  In that way it reminds me somewhat of 4-AcO-DMT, in that everything around you could be melting and distorted, but mentally you're fairly lucid and calm.  However, it's rougher than 4-AcO-DMT for sure.  If you've never taken a DOX, I'd start at 1.5mg, which will be psychedelic but less so than 2mg, for sure.  Any less than 1.5mg will probably produce a sub-tripping state which will be annoying after a while, as it lasts for so many hours.  After I had learned DOC's language, I used .5 - 1.25mg doses as day enhancers a few times and enjoyed it very much, but the first try I attempted was with 1.2mg and it gave me a negative vibe for a while because I got so tired of it.  Also, vodka would be fine for DOC, yes.  Your liquid measurement plan sounds just fine.


Something I experienced with DOC, which may have been due to my experience at the time or other factors, was that the first few times I took it I found it very enjoyable and shocking, but impossible to really use.  For it to reveal its usefulness to me, I had to somehow keep focused during the come-up and beginning peak, or else I would enter what I termed "the divine delerium", where I basically sat around listening to music and experiencing bizarre consciousness phenomena and seemingly reptilian contact which was creepy, while my ego/consciousness was relatively unable to actually assert any sort of control or desire for control.  A strange state which I enjoyed but which I could not figure out how to break through.


Then one time, I discovered a way to keep my mind active.  I believe I came on Bluelight during the come-up and read and responded to posts.  I noticed that time that my mind was able to stay pretty lucid, and I realized that the repitilian consciousness was really my subconsciousness, which I accessed and ended up having an immensely healing and instructive trip.  That's the best way I can explain it.  That was with 3.2mg.


I find DOC to be focused very much on primordial genetic roots and evolutionary material.  it's very "archetypal".  It's really a great substance, one of my favorites.  There's a certain element of euphoria, but it differs from the euphoria of the likes of AMT and 4-AcO-DMT, and that produced by non-amphetamine psychedelic phenethylamines.  It's sort of detached euphoria, with little outright joy.  The exception to this was my healing trip I mentioned above.  During the few hours I was listening to music with my eyes closed, laying down, my soul was just soaring.  It was beautiful.


Music really is enhanced by DOC.  It's as if you can hear the entire song as a cohesive whole, while simultaneously analyzing its separate elements apart from the whole.  Enjoy!

<!-- POST END: id=4836478 -->

*update*

I would just like to report that I think I may have completely screwed up my liquid measurement plan. It turns out I have around 40mg of DOC and not the 30mg I was supposed to get. I am not complaining about that part. I would like to add that it is IMPOSSIBLE TO EYEBALL THIS STUFF. When I first saw how much was in the bag, I thought it looked more like 15-20mg based on my previous experience with other research chemicals.


So here is my problem. I put the ~40mg of DOC into the amber vial and then went to measure the vodka in a 30ml measuring cup (my original plan was 30mg of DOC into 60mg vodka for a 2ml/mg solution) and when I went to put the 30ml of vodka in the vial, an unknown amount spilled (I would guess maybe 5ml)8( . I then measured an additional 15ml of vodka which went in fine. I should have approximately 40mg of DOC dissolved in approximately 40ml of Vodka. 


Does anyone have any suggestions on how to improve this situation? I was thinking of transferring the liquid from the amber vial to another using a syringe and measure it that way and assume a larger margin of error in my solution.


One other question. I was planning on using latex gloves but they proved too cumbersome and my finger did come in contact with a small about of crystals, which I wiped off. I certainly didn't 'pull a Green Barts' and lick my finger or anything, but is it possible I may have 'pulled a Hoffman' and absorbed enough through my finger to trip? I guess time will tell, in the meantime I will skip my regular dose of piracetam just in case...  ![8o](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/eek.gif) 


I could imagine piracetam could have very synergistic (and perhaps completely unpredictable) effects with DOC. Does anyone have any experience with this? I think 800mg of piracetam and maybe 250ug of DOC could be an interesting experiment.


I also saved a little bit of the crystals, as I am intrigued about the reports of people vaporizing DOC, is there any more/new information on that Meth-OD of ingestion?


thanks

<!-- POST START: id=4849905 num=128 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2007-03-19T19:05:57+0000 -->
### Post #128

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4849905 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 19, 2007 at 7:05 PM |
| Page | 7 |

Hmm... I would have re-measured the entire amount of vodka after the spill.  But too late for that now, I guess, huh?


I would assume that what you have it correct and start low.  Be aware that DOC seems quite safe for a DOx and if you're off by even 100% (which I can't imagine you would be close to), you would be fine (although perhaps freaked out!) by a normal dose.


I'm not sure what else to suggest except letting all the vodka dissolve out of the container, and then pouring a new, accurate amount in.  


I have mixed piracetam and DOC close together once, but technically far enough away (3 hours) that it may have had no effect anyway.  In any case, I didn't really notice anything different about the trip except that it was more mentally focused.  I have a hunch (not proof!) that the DOx class is not affected in the same way by piracetam as the 2C-X class, for example (which is affected very strongly in my experience).


If you want to try it, starting with 250ug or so would be a good start.


And I don't think that DOxs absorb through the skin.  I could be wrong though.  I've gotten doc powder on my finger, wiped/washed it off (not immediately), and never felt any effects.

<!-- POST END: id=4849905 -->

thank you very much for this (and your previous) reply. The spill happened on the way into the bottle, so I just had to keep pouring. I think I have things under control, I just should have practiced my technique with something not so rare and potent. I will simply pour the solution from the amber vial into the 30mg measuring cups and then put it back in with the 10ml medicine syringe I have. That should get me within 1ml or so.


As piracetam seems to interact with MDMA and amphetamines I would think the potential would be there for DOC as well. But since the DOx class seems to first accumulate in the lung, where some unknown metabolic process may occur, its over simplistic on my part to assume that because piracetam interacts with *amphetamine, that is will also interact with DOC specifically. I think to test if there is any interaction it would be best to take the piracetam after the DOC, to account for the conversion/accumulation time in the lung before the substance starts to show activity. I think around 250-500ug there could be great nootropic potential.


I'm very glad (but also somewhat disappointed) that my prospects of tripping on an unknown amount of transdermally absorbed DOC this afternoon are pretty low. I do feel something, but nothing that I couldn't attribute to the 500mg capsule of DL-phenylalanine I took, coupled with the placebo effect. If the walls start breathing, then I'll take notice.![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)


*edit*

SO I must not have lost much after all. I measured 45ml of solution from the vial and there was around 7ml of vodka left from the stated 50ml bottle so I must be pretty close. The dosage concentration should be 0.888mg/ml, so to be on the safe side I will assume a 1:1 ratio. My first trial on Wednesday will use 2ml or ~1.8mg, which I feel is a good compromise between 1.5-2 for a DOx virgin.

<!-- POST START: id=4849983 num=130 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2007-03-19T19:42:39+0000 -->
### Post #130

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4849983 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 19, 2007 at 7:42 PM |
| Page | 7 |

After having had a number of incredibly psychedelic and confusing acid-like trips on DOC a while back, complete with amphetamine side-effects (weak ones, but there nonetheless), I now find it to be quite nootropic indeed, and much gentler, with practically nothing amphetamine-related going on in the body except a desire to stay awake for a very long time.  Last time I used it (Saturday night), I took 3.6mg, then 1.5mg 3 hours later.  I stayed up all night, all the next day, and until about 2am last night, with an absolutely racing and whirring mind.  Considering that I get pleasure and saatisfaciton from feeling mentally quick and analytical, it was a great experience indeed!  I felt that it made the flow of words effortless, though somewhat stream-of-consciousness, and I could not help but analyze absolutely everything I saw or experienced.  Just thinking about my weekend has made me near to tears all day, simply because it was so wonderful and bonding for my fiance and cats and I.


Enjoy DOC!  I don't know why, but at first I found it very difficult to get anything from.  I would have these trips where I felt almost taken over by my subconsciousness, and I would be swimming in a bowl of dramatic visual soup all night, the time seeming to snap by and stop at the same time.  I would spend hours staring at something over and over, seeming to communicate with something but without any control over it.


Then I had one trip on it which was also extraordinarily visual and mentally deep, but this one was lucid and crystal-clear and was my best DOC trip.  Since then, I've only used it twice (over 5-6 months), but both times it has been much weaker, not very visual, required a higher dose, and totally mentally lucid and quick.


Actually, any post I made on Bluelight Saturday night or Sunday was while on DOC.  I may go b ack and try to read them to see if my perception of my mental lucidity was true, or a delusion ![=D](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/biggrin.gif)

<!-- POST END: id=4849983 -->

<!-- POST START: id=4933858 num=131 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2007-04-19T16:43:38+0100 -->
### Post #131

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4933858 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |

| Page | 7 |

Last time I used DOC, this past weekend, I had a wonderful trip (I'm planning on writing it up), but I noticed an alarming side effect for the first time: extreme vasoconstriction.  It especially affected my large leg arteries (veins?), and I was unable to stretch my legs all the way out.  My veins in the legs felt like they were so constricted that they'd snap if my legs extended all the way.  When I sat with my legs crossed, I couldn't tell, but walking required hobbling until I'd been doing it for a few minutes, at which point it seemed to stretch them out somewhat.


It was still a great trip with no other side effects, but it alarmed me a bit, especially because it was that strong at T+1:00.  Fortunately, it didn't get worse, but instead got better with time.  it's just odd because I've never gotten more vasoconstriction than a slight bit of pain after just standing up, and I've taken larger doses.

<!-- POST END: id=4933858 -->
