<!-- POST START: id=4944991 num=141 author=VictorBorge author_id=51077 date=2007-04-24T07:00:54+0100 -->
### Post #141

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 4944991 |
| Author | VictorBorge |
| Author ID | 51077 |
| Date | Apr 24, 2007 at 7:00 AM |
| Page | 8 |

Hey everyone! My first post in nearly a year, 's been a while.


This is getting off-topic (bromo-dragonfly vs LSD), but I have to concur with those who say DOC is more than worth trying. I have tripped dozens - hundreds? - of times, on almost everything out there; I am someone who considers psychedelics an important part of my life; and yet I can safely say the only truly life-altering experiences I've had were with three: LSD, DOC and DMT+DPT. 


I could not ever rank the three; they each showed me God, The Universe and Everything in their own ineffable way. But DOC was by far the most spiritual. I spent the better part of 24 hours on DOC weeping and groveling into a dishtowel like an elderly widow, shuddering before the awesome power of God (or whatever you choose to call that Big Thing). 


I'm not a Christian, nor do I proclaim any religious affiliation, but my own nickname for DOC, coined during one of my more lucid moments under its spell, is "Died On a Cross". I felt I could finally understand, to my absolute core, what true spiritual enlightenment was -- and happened to have been reading a bit of Judeo-Christian religious history that week, so there you go. 


But honestly, it all comes down to set and setting doesn't it. I could probably have had the same experience on half a dozen other chemicals, under similar circumstances.


VB

<!-- POST END: id=4944991 -->

Great post and welcome back!


Although DOC was not my most profound trip, it ranked among the top 4 or 5 for sure. Nonetheless, it has still helped me a lot on several occasions and I love it dearly.  I think DOM has the same potential if not more, but the thing about DOC that it wonderful (among other things), is the profound and beautiful sense of sublime peace and joy it instills, especially after the peak and for the next 24 hours or so.

^^^^ While it's often expressed and understood either way, IUPAC nomenclature prefers the first version as it follows proper alphabetic protocol:


4-chloro-2,5-dimethoxyamphetamine.

Question..  The first psychedelic I ever tried was DOC...  I've done it quite a bit and I loved every single trip I've had on it.  Then one day, I was introduced to LSD.  I had done that a few times and had quite a few mind blowing trips on it and hadn't touched DOC ever since..until the other night.  I ingested 2mg (which used to be a good dose for me) and it was awful.  I didn't trip that hard at all and I ended up disappointed.  Could it be that since I tried LSD and it rocked my world that I won't get anything out of DOC anymore, or did I just not take a high enough dose?  I'd like to give it another try with a higher dose but I'm almost scared I'll have a bad experience again.


I've learned a lot from DOC and even had a healing experience with 4mg one time, so I don't want it to end like this...

Is it just me or has DOC fallen "off the radar" significantly lately? Don't get me wrong, this is probably a good thing after all the hype in 2005-2006 but I'm just wondering if people have changed their opinion of it in hindsight?


As for the "astrological sense", I tend to agree, but probably in a different context. I notice my "spiritual energy", "prana" etc. seems to ebb and flow yearly with the solar cycle (peaking around the summer solstice) and my only experience with DOC was ~1.8mg in the spring. I found it uncomfortably stimulating and very electric if that makes sense. It felt a bit as though there was a current of electricity between my joints and it was difficult to get comfortable. The psychedelic effects were pretty minimal and I ended up taking Valium and going to sleep around t +12. I have limited experience with stimulants so I may not have the correct vocabulary to explain myself properly.


Now that its fall and things are starting to wane, I think something a bit stimulating could be useful and I've been contemplating taking DOC again for a while. After a recent mild LSD trip I really enjoyed the length and especially the slow decline.


I think previously my DOCe might have been a bit low so I never really got passed the stimulating qualities. I'd like to try 3mg shortly and see how that works out.


Does anyone know about degradation? I've had my DOC stored in an amber vial dissolved in vodka in the freezer for over 6 months, should I expect any noticeable loss of potency?

<!-- POST START: id=5376459 num=154 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2007-09-28T20:53:44+0100 -->
### Post #154

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5376459 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Sep 28, 2007 at 8:53 PM |
| Page | 8 |

I agree with illusion that DOC feels "astrological".  It's very classically psychedelic, strong, very strong.


My early trials with it were simply fantastic.  For quite a while though it's been much less dramatically psychedelic, and just provided a strongly empathogenic, more weakly psychedelic experience that gives me vasoconstriction.  I suppose this is mostly due to my long-term tolerance which I suspect will be a while to dissipate.  But I wonder if anyone else has experienced the same?


Finally, e1, 1.8mg is going to be a different sort of beast than 2.5-3.5mg.  I'd go for 3, personally.  As long as you're sure you could handle it if it turned out to be too stimulating again (not enjoy, but handle, not freak out).  But personally I find full doses of DOC to be rather relaxing, not stimulating.  My 1.2mg dose of DOC, the first one, was very stimulating, however.  Over the summer, I took several doses of DOC in the 4-5mg range to spend a day with my family and friends in a lakehouse, nortern-Wisconsin paradise.  It was great, just great.  But had I taken that much before, Id've been completely out of commission until about T+10, when the second stage hit.  In fact, now that I mention the "second stage" of DOC, it has seemed every time I've taken in within the past half a year or so the experience has been entirely composed of that second stage, the euphoric, empathogenic, social part.


And from what I understand, DOX substances are extremely stable, like other amphetamines.  I doubt you've experienced degradation.  And also, for what it's worth, the last of the "old kind of trip" that I've gotten from DOC was the last dose I took of the first batch I received.  This batch came as a small collection of small crystals, not as powder, and every experience with it was powerfully deep and psychedelic.  My other DOC has all been of a different appearance, as a whitish-clear powder made of really tiny shards.

<!-- POST END: id=5376459 -->

Also the DOC I got is a very fine crystal, not a powder and I think its from the earlier batches as I got it during the period when DOC was unavailable for the most part.

### Post #157

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5376615 |
| Author | e1evene1even |
| Author ID | 81284 |
| Date | Sep 28, 2007 at 9:54 PM |
| Page | 8 |

Another side note is that during around the time I took the first dose I had also been taking l-tyrosine and DLPA, both likely to enhance stimulation.


One thing I've found to be helpful lately and may be useful with stimulating drugs such as DOC is Taurine. Many people think its in energy drinks because its stimulating, but actually the opposite is true. As a vegan I'm likely a little low in taurine so I could possibly benefit from supplementation in the days prior to taking DOC. I also have a calming amino acid blend with B vitamins, magnesium, taurine, GABA and Valerian, which I'll likely take a few hours before.


I'll also be able to test my hypothesis that a small dose of ketamine, similar to that used in the anti-depressant research would be a good way to ensure a positive mood going into the experience and a less stressful come-up.


> NATURE|Vol 443|12 October 2006 said:
> 			
> 		
> 
> 
> 			So, by jamming the NMDA receptor, could ketamine be correcting a toxic glut of glutamate that is harming brain cells and causing depression? It is already known that stress floods the brain with glutamate, says Zarate. “It might be that these neurons are struggling to regulate glutamate, and if you stress them over and over, they become injured.” This hypothesis is still very new7. There is some evidence linking glutamate, and the NMDA receptor, to depression. Twenty-five years ago, for instance, scientists at the National Institute of Diabetes and Digestive and Kidney Diseases in Bethesda, Maryland, showed that chemicals that target the NMDA receptor have antidepressant effects in animals8. Scientists have since found that deceased depressed human patients, such as suicide victims, have abnormal numbers of NMDA receptors. And brain-imaging studies have found that depressed people have much higher levels of glutamate in one region of their brains than healthy people9.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — NATURE|Vol 443|12 October 2006 said:


> **Taurine**
> 
> L-Taurine is an amino acid that can calm and stabilize your mind much like GABA. By retarding the release of adrenaline, taurine also protects you from the fight-or-flight response and post-stress anxiety. Because taurine is found in protein-rich organ meats, vegetarians are especially at risk for taurine deficiency.
> 		
> Click to expand...


> **GABA (gamma-aminobutyric acid)**
> 
> Reduced levels of GABA in the brain and nervous system are linked to anxiety, tension, and insomnia. In fact, prescription antidepressants like Valium and Librium work by increasing your system's response to GABA. GABA is an important neurotransmitter (chemical messenger) that helps to regulate brain and nerve cell function, producing a calming and focusing effect. GABA also protects the nervous system against overload which can lead to over-excitement or impulsive lapses in judgment.
> 		
> Click to expand...

### Post #159

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5378963 |
| Author | Jabberwocky |
| Author ID | 520884 |
| Date | Sep 30, 2007 at 12:04 AM |
| Page | 8 |

While there is not enough evidence to extrapolate a complete pharmacodynamics for each individual psychoactive substance we are discussing (remember every compound is unique), there is enough research done to generally get an idea of what receptor subtypes they are acting on.


In the case of DOC it is a full agonist at 5HT2a and 5HT2c receptors (serotonin receptors). It causes postsynpatic changes by binding to the receptor and changing the flow of information in your brain.

<!-- POST END: id=5378963 -->

Just to add my experiences to the mix. My most memorable experience with it was a 5mg dose of DOC diluted in ethanol on an empty stomach. The come-up was suprisingly fast since 30-45 min in I was already tripping. The rest of the trip was a magical blur. At its peak I was at an intense +++ for two solid hours. The amphetamine like kick and euphoria was very clean and mellow (which is a rarity for me with psychedelics) and the visual were absolutely amazing. I was almost down about 12 hours after dosing.


As far as the mental activity, i found it very comparable to the maelstrom of confusion and profound insight that comes with shrooms, acid, and other of the more heady psychedelics.

<!-- POST START: id=5449641 num=164 author=e1evene1even author_id=81284 date=2007-10-26T03:23:47+0100 -->
### Post #164

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5449641 |
| Author | e1evene1even |
| Author ID | 81284 |
| Date | Oct 26, 2007 at 3:23 AM |
| Page | 9 |

My first question would be what other drugs you may be taking, including, SSRI's etc. Prior experience with psychedelics and your state of mind (set) before hand can be major factors as well.


Sometimes what can happen, especially with lower doses is that uncomfortable, unconscious material can surface but the dose isn't high enough to 'transcend' that stage and you end up spending a lot of time wallowing in your problems. In the context of psychedelic therapy this can be therapeutic and even desired, but if you are simply looking to 'trip out' and can be quite undesirable.


I've only taken DOC once at 1.8mg and it was similarly uneventful. I didn't experience any depression though.


For the time being, I'd lay off psychedelics and take some time to integrate the experience.


Some great information on handling difficult experiences and general tips for using psychedelics wisely can be found [here](http://www.erowid.org/psychoactives/writings/stolaroff_using.shtml). You may find it helpful

<!-- POST END: id=5449641 -->

Ive never had the absolutely ridiculous thoughts a hard acid/shroom trip will give me from DOC, but that can be seen as a positive as well I suppose.  The DURATION of this stuff is absolutely amazing.  The duration almost kind of knocks it out of regular recreational use, for me at least.  I question I had about it is the form that it comes in.  When I get some its always on blotter paper but a friend said that it actually comes in crystallized form but they put it on blotter to make it easier too distribute. Any info on this?

I've been using this recently (from a relatively recent batch) as a low-dose supplement to my day, sub-psychedelic.  At this dose it is free of any side effects and gives me about 6-8 hours of serious nootropic augmentation, speed of thought, motivation, and drive to categorize and optimize my processes.  Then it begins to shift into the laid-back, euphoric and talkative stage for the rest of the day, which is fantastic.  I have taken such a dose 3 times this week, on Monday, Wednesday, and today.


I've been very loaded down at work lately so I took low doses on those days at about 7:30am before work.  It worked absolutely fantastically.  it provided me with a very nice body buzz and energy without any sort of overstimulation at all.  it gave me motivation and a desire to communicate with my fellow employees, whom I normally try to avoid as much as possible.  Basically it has turned a really hectic week into an enjoyably intense week which I am about to receive two awards for doing such fast and efficient work.


On those days, later on after work I end up spending the whole evening and night with my fiance, having a blast and just laughing a lot and feeling the love very deeply.  It has been one of the best weeks I've had in a while.  And our kitties have been sleeping in the bed with us which they do not normally do, and being even extra snuggly (they are always snuggly but this is ridiculous) ![=D](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/biggrin.gif).  I attribute it to my radiation of an aura of peacefulness and joy.

.5 to 2mg.  Given that I am not as sensitive to psychedelics as I once was.  I may have found it a bit more distracting two years ago, as I used to get more side effects from things.   I would recommend others to try it at .25 to .5mg to start... try to get to a level in which you are only subtly altered, not outright under the effects of the drug.  At the level I am talking about there are no visuals


Also, I should mention I have been well able to sleep each night by midnight, although I also think I could have stayed up all night had I wanted to.

Question:  why did you dissolve any chemicals in denatured alcohol rather than alcohol that you knew was safe?  I would recommend ethyl alcohol, even dissolving it in vodka or something if everclear (nearly pure alcohol) is not available where you are.  I'd use isopropyl alcohol next, as it will evaporate totally and shouldn't contain other things.  Isopropyl alcohol is dirt cheap as well.


Unfortunately I don't know how to answer your question though.  If everything in this alcohol blend evaporates completely, you should be able to evaporate and scrape up the crystals.  If not, you'll have to find some way to remove the poisonous stuff, and be damn sure you got it all.


Finally, regarding DOC's stability... it is a very stable molecule, as amphetamines tend to be.  It could be exposed to air for a long time and be fine.  Stored as crystals or in liquid in a cold, dark place, it would last for years... possibly much longer.

<!-- POST END: id=5568660 -->

I have read that Diethyl Phtalate doesn't dissolve in water. So, I would just evaporate the alcohol in a surface and rre-mix the crystal DOC with distilled water. Only one person has complained about the alcohol and got GI disturbances, but he drank the mixture while the alcohol was still evaporating. How much would I lose this way anyway, by evaporating? I guess not so much but something has to be lost. Thanks for answering so completely, bye.

### Post #194

| Field | Value |

| Post ID | 5592458 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Dec 19, 2007 at 1:12 AM |
| Page | 10 |

^^ I have seen it where it was made into a powder... it may be difficult to tell, but is it a dull white powder (like powdered 2C-Xs for example) or is the powder shiny to some extent?  Powdered DOC forms a dense, shiny powdeer because the crystals are brilliant white, shiny crystalline structures.  In contrast, crystals of the 2C-X class that I've seen are almost like flakes... their appearance is totally different, not at all like shiny, needle-like crystals.


And yeah... don't snort it.  Oral works very well and is a lot less potentially dangerous.

<!-- POST END: id=5592458 -->

Of course it is possible. Nobody has died from an DOC overdose and the LD50 (the dose at which 50% of the population will die) is not established for DOC (this is done with animal testing and extrapolated to humans).

<!-- POST START: id=5794214 num=235 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2008-03-07T21:36:11+0000 -->
### Post #235

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5794214 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 7, 2008 at 9:36 PM |
| Page | 12 |

No, a drop is **way** less than a mL.  There are a lot of drops per milliter.  Once dissolved the chemical will most assuredly be evenly distributed... that's how dissolving works.  You run into problems if a material is not water soluble... then it forms a suspension.  But DOC is definitely water soluble so you won't have to worry about that.


To measure a milliter, go to a pharmacy and buy an oral syringe, or even ask for one behind the counter, and they should give you one for free.  I bought one for a dollar which accurately measures by 1/5 mL increments, so it's extremely accurate to dose in this way.  Really there is no difference between a 1mg/mL solution and a 1mg/100ml solution in terms of safety if you can accurately measure.  In fact it would be a giant pain to measure out 100mL for each mg of DOC... it would probably be less accurately because you won't find a syringe that measures more than 10 or 20mL at a time, and you'd have to fill it multiple times.


But since you have so little of an amount of DOC (your dog rather), maybe you could go with 5mL per mg, or even 10mL per mg, just because 10mL of water is going to look really small in most jars or vials.


Finally, you should put some alcohol in the solution if possible, to prevent bacterial growth and such.  If you have access to everclear, you can use 20% everclear and 80% distilled water (distilled is important, don't use tap for this).  Or if you have vodka, you can use 40% vodka and 60% water.  Both of these will give you roughly 20% alcohol in the solution.  This is another reason for using a small amount of liquid, so that you don't use much alcohol.  You don't want to actually be affected by the alcohol... you just want it to prevent contamination.

<!-- POST END: id=5794214 -->

---

**Anti-addictive effects from DOC**


After my high dose DOC trip the other night, I went from smoking a pack+ a day of camel menthol wides. During the trip, I had ***no*** urge to smoke, and cigarettes still just taste and feel disgustion. I now smoke 4-5 a day, just enough to keep the headaches at bay. The friend who I tripped with made major progress twards getting off of the opiates he loved/hated until that night. The 3rd person we were with (he only took 5mg) was also a heavy smoker until the trip started and has not had a single cigarette since. He crushed his pack and said fuck tobacco. It seems there be a major tool for ridding yourself of negative habbits with DOC. DOC seems a lot more managable and benign than ibogaine.


Has anyone else experienced this after trying DOC???

<!-- POST END: id=5828314 -->

<!-- POST START: id=5829309 num=246 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2008-03-19T13:49:16+0000 -->
### Post #246

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5829309 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 19, 2008 at 1:49 PM |
| Page | 13 |

I stopped smoking before I ever got into psychedelics much, so I can't say specifically.  My worst habit over the past few years has been kratom, and I can't say that it helped me with that, because, well, kratom doesn't feel disgusting like cigarettes do, and it mixes really well with DOC.  However, DOC does produce a state of inner tranquility in me, particularly after the peak, which helps me to be totally satisfied with just myself and the little things in life, which lasts for a good 24 hours at least.  So I can definitely see how it could help with quitting cigarettes.


So how long has it been?  I hope you'll be able to use this temporary reprieve to do some work to prevent yourself from picking it back up. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)  The way I quit was that one day I just realized how crappy cigarettes made me feel, and how much I hated the feeling of them.  So I stopped, and every time I had a craving I just reminded myself how shitty they are.  And then once my tolerance dropped, I started getting nicotine buzzes again if I smoked, and to me, the nicotine buzz is one of the nastiest, most foul feelings in the world.  So it was pretty easy to quit.  I never had any withdrawal symptoms at all.  Just cravings from time to time to be doing the action of smoking.

<!-- POST END: id=5829309 -->

### Post #256

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5838849 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 22, 2008 at 7:38 AM |
| Page | 13 |

There's no way to reliably eyeball any amount of DOC.  The difference between a few milligrams isn't noticeably unless you're looking at two different piles, and even then it's hard to be sure with an amount that small.  You can't remember what 4mg looks like reliably, trust me.  4mg looks different with every powder and even between different piles of the same powder, because of the way the crystals fall.  Your friend is treading on dangerous ground

<!-- POST END: id=5838849 -->

### Post #258

| Field | Value |

| Page | 13 |

**Tingling all over after tripping DOC**


@#$Hey guys/girls/in-betweens so here's the deal: back in February I turned 21 and did a lot of partying with Ketamine. I was doing about a gram a week for like a month and a half interspersed with DOC trips. 


// After the first time I tripped DOC at 3mg, I started getting tingling sensations all over my body, like when your foot falls asleep. It's a very superficial numbness and only occurs on the surface of my skin, there's no muscle soreness or pain or anything. It seems more pronounced when  I come into contact with cold things as well. I don't notice the tingling except when I touch something, like a persons arm, or laying down in bed, or picking up a cup. I originally thought that it was because I was doing what I thought was a lot of Ketamine and that I had a B12 deficiency(comparatively though it doesn't seem like a gram a week is a lot compared to some more hardcore K-heads out there). To remedy what I thought was too much Ketamine intake I took a lot of B complex supplements and  drank a bunch of B12 enriched smoothies. When it first started, the tingling was so bad I actually went to a doctor where they  bunch they did all sorts of shit like testing my reflexes and blood work --all ofwhich all came back normal. 


 The tingling faded and was pretty much gone by a week and a half later and I did some more K where the tingling remained at bay. I waited a few more weeks and then tried DOC again this past weekend and the tingling returned so I'm going to go out on a limb and say the DOC is causing this. 


WTF!!?! I love DOC, it's such a beautiful psychedelic and I really don't like that it's giving me this adverse physical reaction for weeks at a time afterwards. I've worked with this compound several times with doses ranging from 1-4MGs. A few of my friends have also sampled this batch of DOC at doses higher than me and reported no adverse side effects whatsoever. 


Could this be some sort of weird allergy? Does anyone else have similar experiences? What is going on?!?![:(](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f641.png)


EDIT: I also have experience working with DOB and haven't experienced anything like this with that compound either.

<!-- POST END: id=5894260 -->

<!-- POST START: id=5894656 num=263 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2008-04-09T08:12:42+0100 -->
### Post #263

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 5894656 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Apr 9, 2008 at 8:12 AM |
| Page | 14 |

DOC is a vasconstrictor... actually quite a potent one sometimes.  Tingling is just one of the side effects of this.  Whenever I take DOC, I get tingling in the fingers and toes (well sometimes), and I also get very visibly constricted veins, so much so that I will feel the large veins (arteries?) in my legs and arms pulling as I try to fully extend them.  It feels pretty freaky.

<!-- POST END: id=5894656 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6005479 num=266 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2008-05-14T23:31:29+0100 -->
### Post #266

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6005479 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | May 14, 2008 at 11:31 PM |
| Page | 14 |

I took 2mg of this on Sunday, Mother's Day, kind of spur-of-the-moment... I was feeling a call to have some fun, which is pretty much why I took a long break from psychedelics.  For some reason I was expecting it to be like it was when I was doing a lot of psychedelics, that is, not powerfully psychedelic but rather a fantastically long, amphetamine-like euphoria producer.


It came on euphorically, and then around hour 3 it slammed into me and made me start feeling quite self-conscious... I felt strange hanging out with my fiance and cats.  I didn't have a lot to say.  The DOC visuals came into being in my vision very lightly, with patterns subtly swirling, especially clouds.  I felt a bit dizzy whenever I tried to look directly at anything, a curious effect that DOC can have on me.  I had some kratom to try to make myself feel a bit less strange, and it only succeeded in amplifying the dizzy feeling strongly.  From hours 3 to 6 I was quite uncomfortable overall, but it was manageable.  I berated myself for taking a powerful psychedelic spur-of-the-moment, and figured I'd be in for a very long period of discomfort.  I felt guilty for ruining mother's day, as I had to call my mom still, and I was planning to make dinner to celebrate it with my fiance who is a mother to our kitties.


Then around hour 6, maybe 7, the fog lifted, slowly at first.  I started feeling very euphoric indeed, energized, full of insight and emotion.  Everything on the TV became something to joyfully analyze.  I transferred this energy to my fiance and we spent the rest of the day and night having the time of our lives, talking and talking and talking and snuggling and discussing issues.  I achieved the absolutely wonderful euphoria that DOC used to produce in me, a magical feeling of zen-like peace and comfort in living in the moment.  This fveeling stayed with me through Monday as well, and partway through Tuesday.  It has yet to fully dissipate.  Overall I feel that it did me some good... I had been stuck in a bit of a negative place with all the stresses in my life recently and it felt fantastic to just step out of that for a day or two and feel free, and dissect the stresses I have been encountering in my mind without anxiety getting in the way.


And none of that horrible vasoconstriction!


Now I need to make sure not to start using it weekly as a remedy for dealing with life, like I used to.


But I ![<3](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/24.gif) DOC. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=6005479 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6017156 num=272 author=Riemann Zeta author_id=56451 date=2008-05-18T18:19:19+0100 -->
### Post #272

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6017156 |
| Author | Riemann Zeta |
| Author ID | 56451 |
| Date | May 18, 2008 at 6:19 PM |
| Page | 14 |

I think all of the psychedelic amphetamines are vasoconstricting due to their potency and non-selective binding to all of the 5-HT2 receptor subtypes: 5-HT2A, 5-HT2B and 5-HT2C.  The 5-HT2B receptor is found in mainly in the peripheral nervous system and certain 5-HT2B receptor agonists cause nasty cardiac effects, so I wouldn't use the 2,5-dimethoxy-amphetamines frequently.  Come to think of it, I don't know a psychedelic that is not a vasoconstrictor--at least to a certain degree.  The ergoloids certainly are, psilocin and the 4-OH-tryptamines are, the psychedelic amphetamines are.  Perhaps 2C-x compounds are the least vasoactive, but it is tough to consider them proper psychedelics (although I've never had 2C-E and people claim that one is a mindfuck).


To anyone considering taking a 2,5-dimethoxy-amphetamine, keep in mind that they are intense, really fucking intense and are not be toyed with indiscriminately.  You must be absolutely certain of the dose and have a lot of time on your hands.  The trip is long and very fatiguing.  They are not like LSD, where one can trip and wake up the next day feeling like a million bucks, since the trip is so long, you will be tired for a day or two afterwards.

<!-- POST END: id=6017156 -->

| Field | Value |

| Post ID | 6022138 |

**Important question**


a recent batch of DOC was shown to be of low quality, how low has not been quantified. this raises a question about stability of DOx in storage, although they are assumed to be very stable this could be incorrect, or it could be a result of sloppy synthesis, in which case all people working with this material need to inquire as to what the inactive material is composed of and if its safe. perhaps someone with more chem knowledge could give some insight into what possible contaminates would be.


information regarding the dosage of this batch has not come out but i hope BLers will post their findings, with a DOx chem dosage is already tricky WITHOUT an unknown amount of degradation. i encourage anyone working with this material to start low and work with it as if it is their first time. remember with such a potent chem even a 25% potency lose will only change an 'average' dose from 2.5mg to 3.25mg.

<!-- POST END: id=6022138 -->

It's unlikely DOC stored under reasonable conditions will degrade even over many years. However, certain synthetic routes can lead to production of dichlorinated and trichorinated analogs mixed with DOC, likely reducing its potency or even rendering it almost inert...


See:


[http://www.erowid.org/archive/rhodium/chemistry/doc.synth.html](http://www.erowid.org/archive/rhodium/chemistry/doc.synth.html)

<!-- POST START: id=6022600 num=281 author=butane author_id=81341 date=2008-05-20T08:24:34+0100 -->
### Post #281

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6022600 |
| Author | butane |
| Author ID | 81341 |
| Date | May 20, 2008 at 8:24 AM |
| Page | 15 |

The impurities would depend on where they fucked up.  If there wasn't enough chlorine, or of the chlorination didn't work quite properly, there could be some 2,5-dimethoxyamphetamine in there.  Otherwise, as stated above, there could be extra chlorines on there instead of not enough.  If the impurity was a result of improper synthesis, it would almost have to be an amine, as anything else would be removed by even a half-assed chemist.  I can't think of anywhere else that the synthesis could go wrong, so I'm pretty sure any other impurity would have to be intentional.  If so, there's no hope of guessing what it is.

<!-- POST END: id=6022600 -->

### Post #285

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6029079 |
| Author | hamhurricane |
| Author ID | 90682 |
| Date | May 22, 2008 at 6:44 AM |
| Page | 15 |

ok so quick question why is that a tri-flouro group in 2c-tfm would be very active and considerably more potent than the virtually inactive 2c-f, but a trichloro group on DOC would be inactive? is it because of the methyl group in 2c-tfm?

<!-- POST END: id=6029079 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=6030225 num=286 author=butane author_id=81341 date=2008-05-22T17:07:24+0100 -->
### Post #286

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6030225 |
| Author | butane |
| Author ID | 81341 |
| Date | May 22, 2008 at 5:07 PM |
| Page | 15 |

On 2C-TFM, it's a trifluro*methyl* group, like 2C-D with all the hydrogens on the 4-methyl replaced with fluorines.  They're all attached to the methyl, which is then on the 4-position.  It's not a trichloro group that would attach itself to the 4-position of 2,5-DMA during the synthesis, but three chlorine groups attaching themselves to three separate locations.  It wants to go to the 4-position first, but if there's an excess of chlorine they will start replacing hydrogens at other locations on the molecule as well.  I'm not completely certain where, but I'd bet the farm that they'd start filling in the empty spots on the ring (3 and 6) and then, if there were an even greater excess, they might start attaching to the side chain.

<!-- POST END: id=6030225 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6053346 num=294 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2008-05-30T17:04:24+0100 -->
### Post #294

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6053346 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | May 30, 2008 at 5:04 PM |
| Page | 15 |

The visuals are quite LSD-like but I do find them stronger in general.  They differ in quality a bit... hard to explain that sort of thing, really.  LSD's visuals appear more natural, and DOC's are a bit more "neon" (for me at least).


I find the trip quite happy... usually at first it can be a bit overwhelming (depending on dose).  Usually around hour 6 or 8 (depending on dose) I enter the second stage, which is less trippy and more euphoric... it makes me feel so great at that stage.  I can't stop talking and moving around and having ideas.


Definitely expect a VERY long trip (24 hours total is no exaggeration).  You will be tripping strongly for 6-8 hours, and then it will plateau and the plateau lingers on until hour 24 or even longer sometimes, although I always feel quite capable of doing stuff on the plateau, including talking to people and stuff.


It's nothing like tryptamines or any of the 2C-Xs... you're in for a ride.  DOC and the DOXs in general are very, very strong... very immersive substances.  Please do not take it unless you're in a safe setting where nothing can happen for at least 24 hours.  Benzos will only make you a little calmer... they won't kill the trip like they will with weaker substances.

<!-- POST END: id=6053346 -->

### Post #0

DOC's real magic, for me, is in the afterglow I get the day after the trip. My vision is fuzzy and light, colors seem softer and the world just has a carefree feeling. Its such a wonderful experience, very therapuetic if properly utilizied.


Dont get me wrong, though. The actual trip itself is wonderful too ![<3](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/24.gif) 


Ive learned to dose very early with DOC. Usually I wake up a few hours earlier than usual if I plan to trip. The few times Ive done this, though, Ive noticed an extremely acidic like feeling in my stomach if I drink any coffee. It can be quite uncomfortable. So I avoid coffee now whenever I take DOC.


Beautiful substance, need to sample other DOx's now.

^^ Yes, I agree... the afterglow of DOC is my favorite part.  On a low dose it's pure afterglow the whole time.


I have tried DOI, DOB, DOM, and DOT (aleph-1) as well, and none of them really hold a candle to DOC's perfect potential to me, I have to say.  With the rest of them, the aftereffects are annoying, but with DOC, they're heavenly... it's like zen in a molecule.  DOM is more classifically psychedelic, less warm, more transparent... I like DOC's effect on the body... it's all fuzzy and soft.


Great stuff. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)  Took me a while to get the hang of.  If you use it too much it starts to cause really bad vasconstriction... disgusting vasoconstriction in fact, the kind that makes you worry you're going to do some damage.

Coming up there are some festivals I plan to attend. Between my choice of white crystal 200ug blotter and DOC... I am actually much more excited to eat the DOC.


Probably gonna be 3mg next time. Most I ever did was 4mg but I have a feeling that 3mg will be more than enough now that I don't trip nearly as often.

<!-- POST START: id=6305696 num=322 author=Tryptamine*Dreamer author_id=55046 date=2008-08-16T07:43:23+0100 -->
### Post #322

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6305696 |
| Author | Tryptamine*Dreamer |
| Author ID | 55046 |
| Date | Aug 16, 2008 at 7:43 AM |
| Page | 17 |

A lot of people have said that DOC is pretty similar to LSD. After finally trying LSD a few months back, I agree. DOC feels much more like a tryptamine than a phenethylamine, even though it is a phenethylamine. The effects are very similar to LSD, mentally and visually. I've had near total ego loss on DOC and LSD.


DOI and the 2c-x phenethylamines all have somewhat similar visuals, though they affect the mind differently. The visuals I get from DOC are more like LSD's visuals. The body feeling is also sometimes very tryptamine like.


DOC is definitely one of the deeper and most enjoyable of the psychedelics I've tried.


I've also had some pretty dark, scary, and depressing trips with DOC. One trip in particular had me feeling some of the worst despair, sadness, and self-disgust I have ever felt while tripping or sober. It did turn out to be one of my most positive/helpful trips in the end. I did not trip for a while after that one. It somehow left me with a much more positive mindstate for a good while afterward.


> 4-OH said:
> 			
> 		
> 
> 
> 			Also, has anybody experimented with other methods of ingestion ie IM/intranasally/rectally? Any experiences would be greatly appreciated.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — 4-OH said:


I have snorted and plugged DOC. The come up is much faster, full effects within 30min, compared to 2-3 hours for oral ingestion. Plugging and snorting give pretty much the same result. I'd prefer plugging it, as it burns pretty bad when you snort it. You only need 50% or so of your normal dose. Maybe a bit more, but you should start with no more than half a typical dose if you snort or plug. 


The side effects are increased if you snort or plug. I don't get too much nausea from eating it, but I vomited once after plugging it and felt quite a bit of nausea for the first 3 or 4 hours. I've also felt like my blood pressure may have been elevated a bit, though I don't really know. I've never felt that from eating it. My heart rate did not seem to be any higher than usual.


The total duration of the trip seems to be less when plugged or snorted, I'm not sure by how much.


I have also eaten my first dose then snorted or plugged a small amount a few hours into the trip to prolong the peak effects. That did not seem to cause any additional side effects.


I would prefer just eating it, and maybe plugging or snorting 1 or 1.5mg 5-8hrs into the trip to prolong the strongest effects. I don't think the increase in potency or faster come up from snorting/plugging is worth the extra side effects. You are much less likely to have an enjoyable or productive trip if you are distracted by side effects.


With DOC, I usually can't sleep for at least 18-20 hours after dosing. I prefer to sleep late the morning before tripping, then dose close to my normal bedtime. That way, I'll be able to sleep normally the next night. If you dose early in the morning, you'll be up all night and exhausted the next day. I've had no problem with feeling tired during the trip the way I do it.

<!-- POST END: id=6305696 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=6305737 num=323 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2008-08-16T07:57:38+0100 -->
### Post #323

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6305737 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Aug 16, 2008 at 7:57 AM |
| Page | 17 |

> 4-OH said:
> 			
> 		
> 
> 
> 			Hi everyone ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)
> Click to expand...
> — 4-OH said:


If you've never done it before I would be really cautious about this... in fact, it's just a really bad idea to use something for the first time in a situation where you need to act normally.  I do use low doses of DOC in such situations... it's a great chemical for it.  But I'm very experienced with it as well.  It's very strong and it absolutely does not let up.  It leaves social skills pretty intact but it can definitely create that awkward social tripping state, especially if taken unaware.  Generally for me hours 2 to 4 are the most likely to be difficult... after that it starts to level out.  By hour 8 to 10, it should have reached a beautiful plateau.  If possible, I might recommend taking some 8 to 10 hours before the situation you actually want to be in... maybe the night before?  Then you can ride out the afterglow/plateau all day.  In fact I use it like this pretty often at times.


But like I said, you really need to use it in a safe and controlled environment and get the hang of it first.  As has been mentioned recently in this thread, it seems to take people a few tries to really "get it".  It was extremely overwhelming for me the first few times... its character really changed after I had some experience with it.

<!-- POST END: id=6305737 -->

Lately 4mg and 5mg were eaten, spaced 1 weekend apart.


The 4mg trip was slightly stronger than the 5mg trip that was taken the week before.

....


The 4mg trip was combined with MDMA and Ketamine. Great synergy. MDMA mixes with DOC much like it does with LSD, except I felt more focused and "intense" with the DOC. Ketamine mixes well with pretty much any psychedelic if you like Ketamine.


The 5mg trip provided moments of deep insight and watching the ocean, I could see each ripple and wave at once and this formed some pretty cool patterns and a feeling of one-ness with my surroundings.


DOC is also excellent to take with little bumps of Ketamine and go see Deep Banana Blackout :D ... this combo had me dancing like outta this world

It leaves social skills pretty intact but it can definitely create that awkward social tripping state, especially if taken unaware.  Generally for me hours 2 to 4 are the most likely to be difficult... after that it starts to level out.  By hour 8 to 10, it should have reached a beautiful plateau. <!-- POST START: id=6306946 num=340 author=tobala author_id=83055 date=2008-08-16T20:26:43+0100 -->
### Post #340

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6306946 |
| Author | tobala |
| Author ID | 83055 |
| Date | Aug 16, 2008 at 8:26 PM |
| Page | 17 |

Here's the thing, fellas:


Even *if* DOC were to trigger a positive on the initial drug screen, the positive result would *require *a confirmatory GC/MS analysis, in which individual sample (urine, blood, hair) eluents would be compared to known spectra of whatever drugs the examiner would be looking for at that point.


It is *extremely *unlikely that the spectrum of DOC would be included in that spectra list, in fact in all the research I've done on drug testing, it appears that drug testing companies and Medical Review Officers (MRO's) don't--among many other "RC's"--even know what it *is*.


If a positive result *does *come back, then the person being tested must not admit to taking any drugs, and must insist that the confirmatory test be done. A lot of MRO's will blow off the confirmation and attempt to get an admission from the person being tested--because it saves them time and the company money. But one should *never *admit anything to an MRO--and force the confirmation even if he/she knows they're "dirty."


Stick to this strategy and one should--for the present at least--never come up dirty for DOC. ![:\](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/wrygrin.gif)

<!-- POST END: id=6306946 -->

### Post #342

| Field | Value |

| Post ID | 6306981 |
| Author | tobala |
| Author ID | 83055 |

| Page | 18 |

The thing to remember is that--like LEO's, you *never *gain anything by giving information to an MRO. Name, rank, and serial number--that's *it*. If they accuse you of anything, ask for proof and never admit--you won't get in "trouble" for using this strategy.


Thus, your personal life is none of their fucking business so don't feel the need to share. I realize that this is getting into legal and drug-testing issues, but I feel anyone who experiments in their personal time with things like DOC should know this, and in this respect the information is on-topic.

<!-- POST END: id=6306981 -->

Re the worries: your employment is damned important, and your concern is absolutely justified. That's why knowing the rules of the game is so important. But relax, you're gonna be fine... ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

Well the fact that there's an entirely separate test to the amphetamine screeeing to test for MDMA sort of says that anything based on amphetamine  with a degree of ring substitution isn't going to give a positive.


As for admitting anything, I'd go as far as saying never admit to any recreational drug use, but it's useful to know that ephedrine/pseudoephedrine can trigger a false positive for amphetamines, so saying you'd recently had some Pseudofed (as it can be bought OTC without a prescription, they can't peanalize you for using a legal medicine to treat a condition) because your sinuses were congested will force them to either shut the fuck up or do a GC/MS type analysis while not leaving the door open for them to be snidey fucks and imply that you've been taking amphetamines.through innuendo


As tobala said, the confirmation test is a lot of additional expense for them and if you've given a reason for a false positive (never let them know that you know ephedrine can cause a false positive, just ask if it could and let them come to their own conclusions), they're a hell of a lot more likely to just believe that and save the cost of an additional analysis

<!-- POST START: id=6313793 num=347 author=tobala author_id=83055 date=2008-08-19T00:05:51+0100 -->
### Post #347

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6313793 |
| Author | tobala |
| Author ID | 83055 |
| Date | Aug 19, 2008 at 12:05 AM |
| Page | 18 |

Well I for one am of the opinion that you should confront any MRO with a solid foundation of knowing what they're up to. I've snagged *my *knowledge from lurking on forums dedicated to MRO info. They don't like it when guys like me come around, and they even say that they are against using the info on their *public *forums as a means to subvert the drug testing industry.


Thus, I lurk and acquire information, but never contribute because there's no need. In my many hours hanging out with these MD's, I've found they fall into two categories:


1. The type that don't want to see lives disrupted by drug testing. They will listen to explanations for positive results and don't feel good about reporting them. But, of course, it's their job and their concerns are valid when testing truck drivers, airplane pilots, etc. They are skeptical when they send a potential CompUSA employee as positive because who gives a fuck if the guy who's trying to sell you a modem smoked pot over the weekend? The senior mod of a forum I lurk on doesn't even believe that testing for prescription drugs is a good idea because people tend to share prescriptions and he ultimately feels it's a waste of time. Needless to say, I respect and like this individual because he has values that extend beyond generating revenue for an industry...


2. The type who like drug testing as a means of social engineering. These guys are like LEO's in that they don't care if your test is positive for amphetamine because you ingested ephedrine or pseudoephedrine. They exist to validate the drug testing industry that employs them, and will do whatever they can to force an admission of drug use out of you. Don't even cater to them by admitting *anything*. Tell them to *prove *you are drug-positive by providing a GC/MS confirmation. Ask to see it and demand that they prove your result conforms to the spectra that they compare your results to. Trust me, they will go right on the defensive because your lawyer is waiting for them to fuck up, right? ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)


Basically, these guys will behave as LEO's in that they will try to coerce an admission of drug use based on a preliminary screen--i.e., inconclusive evidence. In my opinion, there's no reason to go on the defensive with them, in fact I would come out swinging and say, "Fine, the preliminary test was positive, but let's see what the GC/MS confirmation says. If it doesn't confirm for whatever you're looking for, go fuck yourself."


Don't let an MRO dictate the course of your life. He needs to back up his results with proof via chemical testing which includes a reliable (and expensive) GC/MS confirmation. He doesn't want to do this because he will have to spend more of his time and more of the company's money.


But *make* him do this and act like you know exactly what you're talking about, because if he fucks up you will sue the shit out of him for fucking up your livelihood based on an imprecise preliminary screen.

<!-- POST END: id=6313793 -->

^ Personally I'd treat them with the contempt they deserve if they fell into the second group; not at all difficult to do & get away with if you have a reasonable knowledge of pharmacology & related topics. I had an interviewer try to pull that sort of shit when I went for my teacher training interview because I once had a lump of hash fall out of my lab coat while doing my lab project in the final year of my degree. Obviously somebody there had said something rather disparaging to the TT interview panel and they had me labelled as a major drug fiend (moi? ![=D](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/biggrin.gif)) who should never be let anywhere near a classroom full of kids. Next day they got a letter from me demanding to know what had been said & who had said it with a view to taking them to court for defamation of character and that I'd be seeing my solicitor later that day so they could expect notification of legal action sometime in the near future...


Got a phone call the day after from the TT place that was almost grovelling in its apology for such a thing ever occuring (I still made noises about legal action unless the name of the person who had initiated all this shit was forthcoming for a few weeks, just to make sure they knew I was not to be fucked around with). Of course I never even went anywhere near a solicitor's office, I just knew that they'd royally fucked up by acting on hearsay and decided to make a point. The whole time I was in the teacher training program, nobody ever brought up the subject of drugs with me again, so I must have made an impression (if they'd done a urinalysis, I'd have been a bit buggered, but this was the late 80's and drug testing in the UK wasn't even a glimmer in some twisted fucker's mind ![=D](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/biggrin.gif))

<!-- POST START: id=6320867 num=353 author=Tryptamine*Dreamer author_id=55046 date=2008-08-20T23:45:27+0100 -->
### Post #353

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6320867 |
| Author | Tryptamine*Dreamer |
| Author ID | 55046 |
| Date | Aug 20, 2008 at 11:45 PM |
| Page | 18 |

> 4-OH said:
> 			
> 		
> 
> 
> 			My friend has been hospitalized after taking DOC. He took 3mg and was tripping for 24 hours + and it obviously didn't hold off.  I'm now really worried ![:(](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f641.png)
> 
> Click to expand...
> — 4-OH said:


Do you know how he measured the dose? Most of us do not have a scale or balance capable of measuring such small amounts (I do, though).


If he used liquid measurement, there are a couple of ways the dose could have easily been miscalculated.


1. He could have had a larger amount than he thought. Some people have got as much as twice the amount paid for. If he paid for 100mg and was given 200mg, he would have taken double the intended dose unless he weighed it before dissolving.


2. Some people have tried measuring using drops of liquid, where one drop is supposed to be 1ml or something. In reality, the drop could be 2 or 3 times that. That is not a good way of measuring.


A mistake can easily be made unless the instrument can weigh very small amounts or a known amount is dissolved in liquid and measured very carefully.


It could be that he is unusually sensitive, or just had a difficult trip. I personally think DOC is one of the most physically benign psychedelics out there, but I have had some mentally difficult trips. My first DOC trip was really tough, and that was with a 4mg dose.


I would not worry too much about trying it myself, unless there was some trouble with your friend's vital sign (Blood pressure, heart rate, etc.) measurements at the hospital.


I've checked my blood pressure and heart rate while on a pretty good dose of DOC, and it was within its normal range. I don't think it typically causes much of an increase in BP or HR, unless you are feeling anxious or panicky.

<!-- POST END: id=6320867 -->

| Page | 18 |

I was the one who weighed it out. I weighed 17mg out on a mg scale, and put this in 17 mls of water. I dosed 3.5mg (3.5ml), and the him and someone else 3mg. It just looks like he was extremely sensitive to it, as that was the second time I did it, and the last time I did 2mg.


There was no real need for him to go the hospital, he was just worried and was tripping and thought that was the best idea.

DOC + MDMA is like LSD + MDMA ... but more focused, intense, and "in the moment"...


But it sounds like you're not even sure if you have DOC, let alone the dose. I'd test the waters gradually.. you can always boost a DOC trip by eating more a couple hours after eating a small amount. It's not like LSD where tolerance kicks in almost instantly.

<!-- POST START: id=6356042 num=370 author=nuke author_id=62546 date=2008-08-30T17:47:39+0100 -->
### Post #370

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6356042 |
| Author | nuke |
| Author ID | 62546 |
| Date | Aug 30, 2008 at 5:47 PM |
| Page | 19 |

re: hospitalization

You have to be careful with the DOxs as some people react much differently than others, and to different doses.  I highballed a dose of DOB and then mismeasured which nearly left me in the hospital and dramatically cut down on all subsequent psychedelic use, and I've seen all means and manners of crazy erratic behaviour resulting from doses of 3mg+ with DOI (paranoid delusions, people attacking hospital staff, that sort of thing).  Be careful and if you're new I'd recommend starting around 1.5mg with all the halogenated DOxs.

<!-- POST END: id=6356042 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=6357531 num=371 author=bluedolphin author_id=41559 date=2008-08-31T03:21:12+0100 -->
### Post #371

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6357531 |
| Author | bluedolphin |
| Author ID | 41559 |
| Date | Aug 31, 2008 at 3:21 AM |
| Page | 19 |

Great advice, Nuke. There do seem to be a small but substantial portion of people that get absolutely twisted and possibly delusional on doses that myself and most people I know of who have experienced -- well, in my case just DOI and DOC, of which I love DOC and find DOI boring and bothersome in its duration..


Although I doubt DOC in modest doses is going to cause a seriously life threatening situation even in people who react badly. Unfortunately if people "go the wrong way" on this one it's going to be a long ride. DOC certainly doesn't cause nearly as much vasoconstiction in me as DOI seemed to, and DOB from what I hear is by far the worst in this regard.


DOC feels about as rough on my body as a light dose of clean amphetamine, I believe a solid dose of Xanax could mitigate almost any problem.

<!-- POST START: id=6358334 num=372 author=Percussion_is_Free author_id=65112 date=2008-08-31T09:32:21+0100 -->
### Post #372

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6358334 |
| Author | Percussion_is_Free |
| Author ID | 65112 |
| Date | Aug 31, 2008 at 9:32 AM |
| Page | 19 |

The one time I took DOC, 2mgs, I was unable to sleep for TWO consecutive nights, and even after waking up after the third night (and first night of sleep) I definitely felt the unimistakeable nootropic signature of a tail end DOC trip.  


I'm not a pharmacologist but I think there's got to be an enzymatic difference in some people that makes it a lot toughter to clear this chem from the body.  My girlfriend was sleeping like a baby at hour 14 while I was fully dilated, stimulated, diarhea, +3 tripping.  Also, I have no trouble getting to sleep after acid or MDMA at a normal time--I can slip into sleep while coming down from a roll or acid by taking deep breaths and entering that dream state.  On DOC though, even by night two, I was just way too stimulated.


My advice is, if you haven't experimented with DOC, make sure you have three full days to recover.  I had to call in sick for work, at a job I could handle on acid, no sweat.  The insane head I had on DOC would NOT have allowed me to function in society, though, at all.  I was bonkers.

<!-- POST END: id=6358334 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6364198 num=382 author=lysergication author_id=50535 date=2008-09-02T08:09:57+0100 -->
### Post #382

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6364198 |
| Author | lysergication |
| Author ID | 50535 |
| Date | Sep 2, 2008 at 8:09 AM |
| Page | 20 |

While I find LSD at party to be great and a lot of fun, I'd not say the same for DOC. I find DOC less social and less rewarding in low dose than LSD. You should take in consideration that DOC take ~2h30 to fully come up while LSD take 30'-60'.


I find that the best way to take DOC is in small social setting with 2-3 friends in a beautiful place, dosing pretty high.

<!-- POST END: id=6364198 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=6366244 num=383 author=bluedolphin author_id=41559 date=2008-09-02T23:26:12+0100 -->
### Post #383

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6366244 |
| Author | bluedolphin |
| Author ID | 41559 |
| Date | Sep 2, 2008 at 11:26 PM |
| Page | 20 |

DOC is actually allows me to be more social and coherent than LSD. Once the peak ends and the long wind-down / afterglow phase begins its pretty much party time.


Of course this depends on the dose, how you react, and other factors.


Epsilon, to prepare for DOC I'd prepare almost the same as with LSD. Except give yourself an extra 12 hours before needing to sleep, or have some benzos handy. Personally I can sleep 10-12 hours into DOC and then wake up still tripping lightly, but some people remain wired for as much as 30+ hours after dosing.


Drink water lightly but frequently throughout the trip, avoid caffeine and eat healthy before the trip. You may be like me and find DOC to be one of the smoothest feeling psychedelics.

<!-- POST END: id=6366244 -->

---

Gaian Planes... DOC doesn't feel like any 2C-x or much like mescaline either. I find it far more transparent. The feeling for me is of a calm and focused energy flowing throughout me. I actually find it more comfortable than most LSD trips.


A "smooth dose" for me is any dose I've tried, between 0.2mg and 6mg. I find about 3-4mg to be ideal.

> thenightwatch said:
> 			
> 		
> 
> 
> 			Has anyone tried using DOC for non-psychedelic purposes, i.e. as a nootropic/stimulant/etc.?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — thenightwatch said:


I remember someone saying they took DOC for a long time as a study aid/stimulant.  I think they took lower doses, 1mg and below.  It was here that I read this.  If you search around you might be able to find it.  They said it was pretty effective.


DOC is one of my favorites.  I can only describe the head feeling as mental candy.  I can almost taste it inside my brain, and it is a similar taste to lsd.  I don't know if that makes much sense, but that's the only way I can describe it.  I love the feeling it gives my body.  It is extremely euphoric.  The only downside is that it makes me puke nearly every time, but I prefer to take 6mg or more.  Then again, I always take it in a liquid solution, and liquid solutions tend to make me puke for some reason.  


I would like to try and plug some, or maybe snort it.  Hell, I have even heard of people smoking it.  If that was proven to be safe, I might consider trying it, but I have heard some of the 2c-x compounds can change into carcinogens when you smoke them so I wouldn't want to risk it.


All this talk about DOC makes me want to test it again.  It has been a while, and it is great stuff.  Very similar to LSD IMO, but with more of a body buzz.  Very pleasant though.  It kicks in fast for me.  I feel it within t + 15 minutes, and I am puking by t +30 minutes, 45 minutes top.  It only takes a little while longer to manifest itself than lsd does.  I would like to take some at an event, but the puking has turned me away from that.  I would need to be near a trashcan for the come up.  Maybe plugging would eliminate the purge......dunno.  Only further experimentation will determine the truth.

<!-- POST START: id=6373648 num=396 author=fastandbulbous author_id=59655 date=2008-09-04T23:39:08+0100 -->
### Post #396

| Field | Value |

| Post ID | 6373648 |
| Author | fastandbulbous |
| Author ID | 59655 |
| Date | Sep 4, 2008 at 11:39 PM |
| Page | 20 |

> 2c-bmine said:
> 			
> 		
> 
> 
> 			7 mgs up the nose...yeah it burned...i dug the visuals...the body high wasn't anything amazing. Lasted for literally 15 hrs peak mode...id prolly do it again
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — 2c-bmine said:


I have to say that 7mg of DOC nasally sounds like an irresponsible act - not only will the peak from 7mg be extremely intense (phenethylamines don't seem to follow a linear dose-effect relationship, 2C-E being one of the more noticable compounds exhibiting this * ), but the come up would be far faster and likely to really unsettle most users. Anybody with no/limited experience with DOC should not exceed 2mg and stick to oral ingestion or there's a more than significant risk of becoming one of Erowid's train wreck trips (remember if it goes bad, you're locked into it for a good 10 hours minimum, longer than just about any other commonly available psychedelic)


* - going from 15mg to 20mg with 2C-E is a world of difference, so when you consider that a fully active dose of DOC is 1-1.5mg, taking 7mg is just asking for trouble in the unfamiliar user (5x the fully active dose of 2C-E ie around the 75mg mark is a nightmare waiting to happen)

<!-- POST END: id=6373648 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6384723 num=406 author=bradoi author_id=108029 date=2008-09-08T14:45:24+0100 -->
### Post #406

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6384723 |
| Author | bradoi |
| Author ID | 108029 |
| Date | Sep 8, 2008 at 2:45 PM |
| Page | 21 |

The first time I did it, I took what I thought to be ~1mg (in 1ml H2O/ethanol/DOC solution) to test the waters, and there were no effects to speak of.


It might be that I had made the solution too weak - I was aiming for 1mg/1ml, but I don't trust my scale too much so maybe I was a bit too conservative. Anyway, the 2nd and 3rd time were done with the same solution. 


Second time - around 5 days later - 2ml at around 9:00 in the morning. Waited until about 12, and when nothing much had happened took 2ml more. Now this worked ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png) A very mild and pleasant trip, came in waves and lasted until sometime early in the next morning. Tracers, patterns on walls moving in strange ways, etc. The exploding stars were really nice to watch ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)


Third time - 3 or 4 days after the second time - 5ml of said solution around 10am - tracers for several hours, but nothing more... Went to sleep around 1-2am with no problem. A buddy took the same amount at the same time, with no effects whatsoever, according to him.


I was even doubting if this might have been something other than DOC, but the length of the first (successful) trip, I think, should pretty much confirm that it is real. Also, I'm sure there was some sort of tolerance because of the short time between trials, and also cross-tolerance with a number of other substances... (methylone, butylone, mdpv, mushrooms, weed, alcohol...) - not taken at the same time of course, but on consecutive days. Lack of sleep could have contributed as well. It was a case of "too much stuff to try out, too little time". 


Now I'm waiting for a suitable time to take the last 5ml of the solution. Hoping for a stronger experience this time. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=6384723 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6423826 num=407 author=senzou author_id=94186 date=2008-09-21T11:25:50+0100 -->
### Post #407

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6423826 |
| Author | senzou |
| Author ID | 94186 |
| Date | Sep 21, 2008 at 11:25 AM |
| Page | 21 |

about two months ago i had my first DOC trip, dosage would be 2mg, maybe a bit less.


it was about 2am in the morning when i did it and i had some amphetamine and some beer before (i know, not the most responsible thing to do, but it was a caught-in-the-moment decision and i knew this would be the last opportunity to do it for the next weeks because of my work)


i also had a sitter, who only had amphetamines and some pot. 10mins after ingestion we decided to go to the 24h-shop to get something to drink. i made the fatal mistake to forget my keys (i dont attribute that to the DOC, 10mins in would be too short for that) and well it was middle of the night, my sitter living too far away to be an option to drive to and it was cold.

so there i was, middle of night, no way to get that frickin door open and coming up on a very potent psychedelic i never had taken before. murphy someone? ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

as i didnt wanted to pay the nightshift-fee for some lock-emergency service we basically had to wait there for like 4-5hours.

so yeah, some fucked up setting there ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)


anyway, i felt the first effects about 40mins after ingestion and i think at T+90M i had the first visual effects.


three hours into it i reached the peak, or more a plateu, which then lasted for about seven hours. It was a pretty solid ++ experience, allthough i guess the setting somehow dampened the strength somewhat.


at about T+17h i reached the point where i could say "ok this is finished now" but still it kept me from falling asleep so i had to take a few benzos (had only lorazepam at hand which doesnt work that good for falling asleep for me) but then sleep was no issue, woke up slightly exhausted but no real hangover (apart from the benzo hangover) after some 12h sleep.


did i like it? yeah pretty much, the setting was not exactly helpful for my mood but i had no real problems with it as i found that it gave me some quite profound mood-lifting buzz and body high which actually reminded me a bit of methamphetamine (had that only 3 times in my life in lowish dosages).

the psychedelic headspace was kindof *fluffy* (for a lack of a better word for it) and the visuals were pretty and sortof stylish to look at. 


what i also really liked was the real smooth slow but steady comeup, you dont get jumped at and have all the time to slowly find your way into the experience, id go as far to say that of all the psychedelics i did in my life (quite a few 2c's, all the "oldschool"-tryptamines) this has the best comeup-phase.


what i didnt like was the the duration, the plateu was just like 1-2hours too long, i got tired of that "psychedelic stimulation" in my head but just when i was about to seriously enter the "ok, this sucks!"-headspace it entered the "second phase", the long and slow but steady comedown, which was really relaxed and chilled. at the end though i kind of crashed a bit, not really mental, more like total exhaustion (it reminded me of the meth-comedown as well).

allthough i think i felt some vasoconstriction and had some chest pain issues, but these might have been psychosomatic, allthough the benzos i did at the end did not really made it better, which i would expect if it had been psychosomatic.

i also think that the fact i was already up almost one day before i ingested it and that i did some amphetamines before might have contributed to it, especially considering that my lifestyle is not the healthiest and at that time did alot of amphetamine at least once a week, including the FR->SU up and running and dancing and going to work chore.

i would be interested if someone else had this combination as well and could comment on that.


would i do it again? yes. but not in the near future, probably not even this year. and also i'd do it sober in the morning after breakfast, looks like the way to go with this substance for me. next dosage would be 2,5mg methinks.


uh, got quite large this post, and is probably the first trip report i wrote for like nine years ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=6423826 -->

**DOC and xanax, I have an idea that im hoping you can help with?**


Ok, well ive always had alot of fun on psychedelics and even the trips that were a little hard at times were still wicked trip at other points in the trip. But last friday I tripped on 2C-T-7 and it was unlike any other trip ever and was really scary. I dont know if I took too much, if my mindset had something to do with it or thats just how 2C-T-7 and if thats the case then I definitely dont like T7, If I had xanax things probably would have gone much better but I was too far gone to walk 50 metres away to get a xanax off my friend. Ill add that im not new to psych's, high dose LSD(thatproduces a much strong but much more comfortable headfuck and visuals) is something I love, Salvia didnt phase me but I still liked it, done mushies, ketamine, DXM, 2C-I which I loved and thought T7 would be more like 2C-I but it was nothing like it at all(except slighly similar body load but that wasnt the problem with T7)


BUT, I want to try DOC sometime in the near future and I dont want any experiences like I did with T7, I want it to go as well as possible. So I was thinking if I have a decent supply of xanax and took it along with the DOC would I still trip albeit much much milder and different or will it basically pointless?


Ill just say that im NOT looking for a special experience that is spiritual or too introspective, im just looking to test the substance and maybe get a few visuals and have a little fun with a very mild to non-existant headfuck.


It'd be good if someone could compare any of the drugs out of 2C-T-7, LSD, DOC and 2C-I. I dont meen compare them all to each other(although if you can that'd be great) but just one drug to the other in terms of intensity, visuals, mindfuck or introsepctive qualities, body load and general enjoyment.


Thanks a bunch to all you guys, im getting so much more interested in psychedelics rather than shooting up hard drugs everyday like I was used to, so thx ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

If you are looking for descriptions of the drugs the best way that you can find them is to read a bunch of different trip reports and information on here, Erowid, and elsewhere. But bottom lnie, it is a very individual thing. We really can't decide what drugs YOU should take, nor should we, that is an individual decision to be made in full knowledge of one's own chemistry, psychology, and the drugs one has at hand, etc. Good luck, though, in your quest to find "something better ..."

It was pretty dumb of me to do the T7 coz I did about 2 days research and the rest was just little bits of info gathered over the years.

^ Ah well, we all have those bad experiences that help us become more mature and responsible drug users along the way. 


Sometimes I'm unable to resist the urge to trip, even if my mindset isn't the best. ![:\](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/wrygrin.gif)


> It'd be good if someone could compare any of the drugs out of 2C-T-7, LSD, DOC and 2C-I. I dont meen compare them all to each other(although if you can that'd be great) but just one drug to the other in terms of intensity, visuals, mindfuck or introsepctive qualities, body load and general enjoyment.
> 		
> Click to expand...


I've had DOC on tabs a few times recently, it was less intense then acid but still intense... hard to explain, there was less of a mindfuck perhaps? The visuals were different as well, they were more intense then the ones I get from acid, a lot of patterning over my vision which at night made it hard to see. I don't really get introspective trips so can't comment there... the bodyload was quite stimulating, a bit too much sometimes but I felt really nice and overall each of my three trips has been great, a really enjoyable experience that I didn't have to 'work' for to get euphoria out of.

**Alternate methods of ingesting liquid solutions**


So I have DOC suspended in a liquid solution at 2mg/ml. I'm kinda tired of the time-frame  involved in tripping on DOC, so I have been thinking about insufflating/plugging a small amount of liquid. For reference, there is no alcohol in the solution, it is being stored in a cold environment for a short period of time.


Anyone have any experience with either of these methods?

Just drink it.  You could plug it.  A slightly lower dose would be needed, dunno how much less though.  


Snorting it would be pretty hard.  You could empty it onto a pyrex plate and let the liquid evaporate, and snort what is left, but it will be such a minuscule amount it will be hard to retrieve.  You will probably end up losing the dose.

<!-- POST START: id=6614871 num=421 author=andymac08 author_id=85420 date=2008-12-05T19:53:39+0000 -->
### Post #421

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6614871 |
| Author | andymac08 |
| Author ID | 85420 |
| Date | Dec 5, 2008 at 7:53 PM |
| Page | 22 |

After plugging it, the only differences I noticed were an extremely fast comeup (significant effects within 5 mins) a MUCH quicker onset of the peak, and length of peak, and totally down buy 12 hrs, which for me is significantly shorter, but only by about 6 hrs or so...


All in all, worth doing, peak was MUCH more intense than equal amounts orally, but that could be just from the speed and slightly potentiation....Probably won't repeat.

<!-- POST END: id=6614871 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6640200 num=422 author=ManRider author_id=106699 date=2008-12-14T03:12:14+0000 -->
### Post #422

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6640200 |
| Author | ManRider |
| Author ID | 106699 |
| Date | Dec 14, 2008 at 3:12 AM |
| Page | 22 |

Yesterday I tried DOC for the first time at a dose of 4mg, and I was mostly at a moderate +++, at least for the peak of the effects. 


I enjoyed the trip overall, especially the strong visuals and other sensory effects, but I felt that it lacked any sense of spirituality, or mysticism, and it didn't even stimulate my thought process very much. 


Compared to other substances I've used like mushrooms, lsd, and 2c-e, DOC was enjoyable but it just made me space out and enjoy the imagery, as opposed to enjoying the imagery while thinking about things or having clever dialogue with my friends. Does anyone else that has tried DOC feel this way about it as well? I haven't seen anyone really mention this aspect of it one way or another.

<!-- POST END: id=6640200 -->

<!-- POST START: id=6892388 num=427 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2009-03-01T00:42:22+0000 -->
### Post #427

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 6892388 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 1, 2009 at 12:42 AM |
| Page | 22 |

I find DOC to be a powerful tool for channeling positivity and love and creativity, when used right.  The afterglow (actually the entire trip when a low dose is used) reliably puts me in a "state of grace" where I feel truly cognitively enhanced, and emotionally honest and open.  It's a zen-like state of peace and harmony where I feel that anything is possible.  My wife and I have had some very important growing days/discussions in such a state.  It's difficult for me to explain this state, but the more experience I have with it, as long as I don't overuse it, the more reliably I can bring it on.  About 1.5 to 2mg works the best, I find.  It just makes everything so positive and easy and "flowing".


I have tried DOB, DOC, DOI, DOM, and DOT (aleph-1), and DOC is the only one that produces this state for me.  It's been a very valuable tool for me, one that remains valuable.  Not as a way to trip balls or hallucinate (it used to do a great job with that but no longer does), but as a way to open myself up mentally and emotionally in an honest and productive way.

<!-- POST END: id=6892388 -->

^interesting.


I've only tried DOC once (~1.8mg) and I found the stimulation uncomfortable, but at that point I hadn't any experience with stimulants (aside from caffeine that is).


Over the last year or so I've been using desoxypipradrol and modafinil periodically and find them to be very useful productivity enhancers.


I think my body has become much more comfortable with stimulants so I think its time to go back to DOC.


I'm hoping low dose DOC can provide a similar 'enhancement' as these milder stimulants, but with a little extra 'magic' if you know what I mean...
