<!-- POST START: id=9701953 num=778 author=IamMe90 author_id=176120 date=2011-06-03T18:18:07+0100 -->
### Post #778

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9701953 |
| Author | IamMe90 |
| Author ID | 176120 |
| Date | Jun 3, 2011 at 6:18 PM |
| Page | 39 |

Well, in a stupid careless mix up I somehow had miscalculated how much i had put on, as in made a simple mathematical error while dosing with the syringe. looking back at the numbers and the intensity of the trip its clear i dosed about 13mg instead of 3-4 i had intended. i hadn't intended to dose it but i got irrationally nervous carrying the thins through security and decided, since i'm well acquainted with 3-4mg doses (which tend to leave me completely mentally lucid) that i would just eat them. 


cross posted from somewhere else (i might turn this into a full TR sometime soon): 


It was probably the most visually intense trip I've had in a good while (only being surpassed by my 2c-e and LSD experience), and the DOC became a REAL (as in, included aspects that I find fundamental to a worthwhile trip, difficult ones - extremely altered mindset/thought patterns, etc), bordering on ego loss at times... all while in the fuckin airport trying to catch my flight lol. I had to throw up in the airport bathroom, which was exciting to say the least.


However, after my initial rough come up, the trip was absolutely incredible. Watching the clouds and the ocean morph color and shape constantly in beautiful synchronicity was awe inspiring - i had the feeling the entire time "this is a once in a lifetime opportunity - most people wouldn't think to trip during a flight, because it's risky, but i'm saeeing some of the most beautiful things i could ever see and wow!" My CEVs were leagues above any high dose LSD experiments and were right on par with 2ce


The bad parts though, were really bad. I could barely see in front of my face from all of the flying synesthetic visuals barraging me in the airport - combined with the crippling nausea and the panic at what I had done was really disorienting, especially while trying to get through security and onto my flight. God, what a fuckin journey ahha

<!-- POST END: id=9701953 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9707263 num=784 author=JBrandon author_id=138901 date=2011-06-05T06:13:59+0100 -->
### Post #784

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9707263 |
| Author | JBrandon |
| Author ID | 138901 |
| Date | Jun 5, 2011 at 6:13 AM |
| Page | 40 |

I need to find some way to reduce the muscle tension before I take this again. I felt like I was candyflipping, which was great, but within ten seconds of peaking I realized my back and jaw were going to be in for a world of hurt later.


I've never caught myself grinding so hard and I could not get the tension in my back to release, no matter what I did. Stretching, rolling around on the floor, nothing I did changed it.


Also I found this to be a really selfish drug - I never felt a sense of connectedness or oneness. There was no transcendence or profound insight at any stage.


Currently I'm thinking this one is more of a fun drug or sex drug.


I was only at 1.5mg, and I was in the worst possible setting I could be in, but I can't even imagine what my body would have felt like at 2.0mg. I feel like I would have no teeth left and my spine would be broken.

<!-- POST END: id=9707263 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9707334 num=786 author=JBrandon author_id=138901 date=2011-06-05T06:59:48+0100 -->
### Post #786

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9707334 |
| Author | JBrandon |
| Author ID | 138901 |
| Date | Jun 5, 2011 at 6:59 AM |
| Page | 40 |

Based on my experience, I feel like your thoughts would become so manic and frenzied it wouldn't be possible to hold onto a single insight or thought at that dose. There is a good TR on Erowid where someone takes 15mg and he basically winds up in a curled up ball on the sidewalk for 8 hours.


Also, at 1.5mg, I was done with all effects by 10-11 hours, and in fact falling asleep.


I was completely done with any psychedelic / visual / stim effects by 8-9 hours, but I had a minor "fog" that didn't clear up until 10-11 hours post-dose.


I was stunned at how short the trip was, TBH. The come-up took 2-3 hours, plateau was about 3 to 4 hours and then it was a steady and smooth comedown from there until 8-9 hours after dosing.

<!-- POST END: id=9707334 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9749012 num=801 author=clubberdude author_id=184317 date=2011-06-19T04:28:57+0100 -->
### Post #801

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|

| Page | 41 |

I tried DOC for the first time tonight (its my first experience with any of the DOX compounds) and all I can say is WOW!!!!!!! 


This compound is very odd indeed! It is by a wide margin the most visual compound i've ever tried, yet, despite the almost sensory-overload visual aspects, my mind is so very clear - I could easily program a computer or solve a complex technical problem in this state. Its really very odd how one aspect (the strength of the visuals) can combine with the super-enhanced level of clear headedness, compared to a day-to-day state.


This chemical reminds me greatly of 2C-P but feels far cleaner - almost like a refined version of 2C-P. A far higher Signal:Noise ratio it seems.

DOC reminds me greatly of LSD except it's got more of a strong, physical push which can be extremely euphoric.  it lacks the nasty body load that other DOXs can have. > — Xorkoth said:


For the record, I have found DOC to have vastly stronger visual effects than LSD - where the visuals for me are relatively subtle. Also DOC is more euphoric - has a degree of unadulterated, carefree bliss than many of the tryptamines can be.


I'd have said that the visuals that I've got of DOC are very similar to the imagery seen in this video. Certainly seems to be in that order of complexity.[http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=T19M9JQFERU](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=T19M9JQFERU)

Now that things have died down and people have gotten to experiment with this a few times is it worth stocking up on considering it's not often available but now is?

I'm considering getting a few doses and just having them stored in a vial for in the future - it's unlikely I'll dose often due to the long duration.


How is the chemical itself though? To be honest, I'm only really a fan of the standard psychedelics like LSD/Psilocybin because the likes of the 2Cs carry far too many side effects for what they are worth in comparison to say acid. Is this a good clean psychedelic like LSD with little side effects - I'm not comparing it to LSD visual/headspace wise, more so does it give bodyload, nausea, etc; for example 2c-e is definitely going to make me sick. I personally find RCs only really worthwhile if I can't get my hands on the standard textbook drugs, but this one has been around for a long time and sounds interesting. 


Would I be better waiting for another DOx to come around? How does it fare in comparison to them?


- Few questions there, hope some people can answer, even just a single one.

I took 2.5mg of the purple-ish tinted DOC and experienced a pretty janky bodyload the entire time, it was absolutely exhausting. I couldn't find any benzos for a while and it was very taxing existing in that state. Finally a friend got me 3 ambien (only thing he could find) and those helped the body load for a few hours a piece but even with those I was worn very thin by the end of the trip. I've took a handful of the 2C's and enjoyed them all very much and could easily tolerate the bodyload but this stuff didn't agree with me at all. I was very excited for this one too ![:(](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f641.png)

<!-- POST START: id=9762470 num=816 author=clubberdude author_id=184317 date=2011-06-23T12:37:58+0100 -->
### Post #816

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9762470 |
| Author | clubberdude |
| Author ID | 184317 |
| Date | Jun 23, 2011 at 12:37 PM |
| Page | 41 |

Body load isn't really any worse than that with 2C-P or LSD, but I noticed what might have felt like some mild vasoconstriction during the time I took it, but this may well have been imagined. I took 4mg orally, and insufflated a total of around 2-3 mg several hours later. The vasoconstriction feelings did not begin until a short while after insufflating the second dose. My heart rate was surprisingly low during the peak of the trip - within around 5 bpm of my typical resting heart rate. At these doses, whilst the visuals were very strong, I felt pretty in control throughout. In fact effects were milder than I expected from that dose, but may have been because I used MDMA the night before.


Next time i'll dose fully orally, as it seems potentially safer. There is absolutely no safety or toxicity parameters about DOC anywhere on the internet, so its best to start out carefully with this one.


My batch is the one with the purple tinge to it.

<!-- POST END: id=9762470 -->

Tried 8 mg DOC 3 days ago.

Weight : 45kg

Height : 1m66-68


What a crazy ride. Very funky psychedelic and long lasting! Bodyloads are mellows, experiences some tension & spasms. Slight increase in heartbeat & blood pressure. Bodyloads are not very strong compared to DOI.


Sweet stuff i love it ! (Beware 8 mg was INTENSE!, i'm experience with DOI up to 6mg so for me it's "easy" to keep cool on DOC).


Peace, be safe!

<!-- POST START: id=9774968 num=829 author=IamMe90 author_id=176120 date=2011-06-27T15:20:17+0100 -->
### Post #829

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9774968 |
| Author | IamMe90 |
| Author ID | 176120 |
| Date | Jun 27, 2011 at 3:20 PM |
| Page | 42 |

Consumed 7mg of the purple tinted DOC, dissolved in distilled water. 


Observations: Experienced the same type of body load as before - persistent nausea on the come up, once I purged myself very minimal body tension and virtually nothing else.


Conclusion: The purple tinted DOC is the same as the white DOC I have previously experienced. I can't believe people thought that somehow this purple batch was some "super potent" DOC or something... come on now. 


The trip:


A fun, tumultuous and totally heart-strain night! 


t + 0: DOC taken. Feel faint nausea and anxiety mere seconds after ingesting, psychosomatically induced symptoms I assume. 


t + 30: Feeling very faint effects, visual and auditory, nausea has not become pronounced yet so I take a shower. There is no music playing, yet I feel very musical and sing some of my favorite Beatles songs with no accompaniment and don't miss a note. This is a very musical drug. 


t + 50: Purged. That felt good. I am engulfed in quite a fuckton of fractals and loving it. Getting the phenethylamine "fan effect," where it looks as tho a fan is blowing very high speed across the ceiling - I get this on 2c-e as well. Very much enjoyed, but we have to turn the actual fan off because it's a bit much, haha. 


t + 2: The night gets interesting. I am with one other person on DOC (5mg), and 4 others on low dose mushrooms. We are feeling a bit "loki the prankster" tonight and decide to shake things up a bit, because that needs to be done sometimes. We go to a large field whilst peaking and light $200 worth of good fireworks off in one haphazard explosive device. We give the national Mall a run for its money. Then the night gets *really* interesting. Three vans, who we now presume to have been irate neighbors masquerading as cops, circle around us very pointedly in the field, closing in on us. At this point we book it at break neck speed in pitch black to the car and make it out fine, like we knew we would... but it was still quite exciting anywho. I haven't had a perceived LEO chase in a long, long time lol, early high school days.

<!-- POST END: id=9774968 -->

| Field | Value |

I would caution against that high of a dose. My 2C-x tolerance didn't appear to have anything to do with my reaction to DOC. I am fairly hard-headed when it comes to the 2Cs. However, I'm very sensitive to amphetamine, and man oh man if my DOC experience wasn't more in line with that.


I'd try 2.0mg at the most for a first time. You won't be bored.

<!-- POST START: id=9786373 num=843 author=JBrandon author_id=138901 date=2011-07-01T04:51:46+0100 -->
### Post #843

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9786373 |
| Author | JBrandon |
| Author ID | 138901 |
| Date | Jul 1, 2011 at 4:51 AM |
| Page | 43 |

Look, Pihkal/Tihkal doses may be "low" but I bet his purity was consistently higher than an Indian/Chinese lab where no one is regulating production.


If you're playing with DOC, don't be swayed by the higher dose reports for your first time. Start low. I'm not saying it isn't fun or rewarding at a higher dose, but you don't know how you're going to react. Look at how all over the place the TRs are for this stuff. I think there may be some measurement issues (shit scales, etc.) but still...

<!-- POST END: id=9786373 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9789900 num=850 author=longtimesunshine author_id=197281 date=2011-07-02T08:19:59+0100 -->
### Post #850

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9789900 |
| Author | longtimesunshine |
| Author ID | 197281 |
| Date | Jul 2, 2011 at 8:19 AM |
| Page | 43 |

i had the pleasure of trying doc for the first time about a week ago. i took 5 mg pure doc (split 10 mg with my brother) and slipped into the most INTENSE comeup of any substance i'd ever experienced...about 3 hrs in length. once i got past that bitch of a tweaky, nauseous, high-speed rollercoaster through hell, it was a glorious ride. what a SWEET fucking drug. i was tripping my balls off with geometric shapes and patterns behind every object, somewhat comparable to the intensity of the hallucinations with 4 hits of really good acid. also, the euphoria that went along with it was strong and present the whole time. yes, this drug truly lasts a full 24 hours and even a little more if you take a higher dose as in my case. 


also, regarding the amount needed to trip- i do believe that 2-3 mg would be a very enjoyable and manageable experience, but because most of the people posting on this forum are very well versed with psychedelics, a much higher dosage is still possible to control...and way more fun :D 


but seriously...doc was way cool, and i'd definitely do it again EVEN though i couldn't take in food for a full 8 hours after ingestion without hurling it up suddenly and violently 30 mins later haha. that was the worst part but can totally be prevented next time. idk if that was just me, but i'd suggest to just eat beforehand to avoid the possibility ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

I second that. Although I did take 7mgs (and it was reasonably intense, though totally manageable), I did use MDMA the night before (and theres likely some degree of cross-tolerance there), and I regularly take an SSRI, so probably some degree of serotonin downregulation is at play, increasing my tolerance to both Phenethylamines, and in particular, Tryptamines. I gauged increasing the dose carefully according to how I felt.  


Dosing low for a first attempt is pretty important here because of the long duration of the chemical. That said, I found it mentally pretty forgiving (see my trip report on DOC), and there was an immense state of calm during the trip.


To add to the point above, 97% purity is pretty good - that means 5mg of powder will contain 4.85mg of DOC, which is a barely significant difference.

<!-- POST END: id=9792931 -->

Yes, if you want a 0.5mg/ml ratio then you want to make the final volume 40ml. So 20ml distilled water + 20ml alcohol is recommended. I use vodka for my solutions, which is 40% alcohol, or 2:5 ratio of alcohol to water. This is plenty to prevent bacterial growth.

<!-- POST END: id=9844959 -->

I also use same ratio as Survived Abortion. Vodka. (Trojka if you want to know).


DOC, people seem to like it a lot, the ratio of positive vs negative experiences (p/n) is quite high, and I am quite happy to see that, because we are going to try it soon. I already tried 1mg dose, quite euphoric and humoristic mental space I must say. A lot like LSD but still not quite it - LSD is very sharp and direct, very clear headed, while DOC is quite soft on both mind and body, also clearheaded. I tried LSD only one tab, and DOC 1mg, separately. 


I have to add I have tried 2c-i, 2c-e, 2c-c and 2c-p and many other non psychedelic drugs, and I find only 2C-I and 2C-I+2C-C combo worth ingesting. I am not visual person (I don't hallucinate much), but I appreciate body load, mental space and euphoria from those drugs. I cannot rate visuals because I do not get them ![:!](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/argh.gif)

 so idk man maybe youre shits weak...?that sux- wish it wasnt against the rules to share. it shouldnt take more than 4mg, at the most, for a phenominal experience IMO.

<!-- POST START: id=9848881 num=880 author=Solipsis author_id=91690 date=2011-08-03T21:02:56+0100 -->
### Post #880

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9848881 |
| Author | Solipsis |
| Author ID | 91690 |
| Date | Aug 3, 2011 at 9:02 PM |
| Page | 44 |

> [IamMe90 said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9848800)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I'm not so sure if just because a drugs duration of action is twice as long, means that you can conclude it's tolerance will last doubly long. I mean, does mushroom tolerance take only half or two thirds of a week to decrease rather than the standard week?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — IamMe90 said:


I don't think it's established or clear to assume that it would be the duration of exposure that influences tolerance. My suggestion is that it is first of all the affinity, which consequently influences the needed dose. For a number of potent phenethylamines it might seem like there is a correlation between affinity and resistance to metabolism (the latter of which is critical for duration of effects), but the NBOMe's are a fine exception to the rule. Apparently because of the cleaveable bomamine group. That amine is an important site for metabolism and almost all other psychedelics show variation in the structural formula in other parts of the molecule.

Looking at these NBOMe's and at DOX compounds as well we can infer that the affinity is what measures the extent of effects on receptors, which makes sense since a great affinity means a good fit (although there still has to be receptor activation otherwise you end up with an antagonist) and including the effects on the receptors can very well be tolerance from upregulation.

LSD has a high affinity but I think it acts strangely and as a sort of partial agonist if I'm correct, also cascade effects are from what I remember thought to be responsible for what it does so it may not fall into the same rules.


DMT shows us though that the exposure can be so very short that whatever the affinity is there is just hardly an opportunity to cause upregulation. I expect oral DMT to produce tolerance, never really thought about it or heard about it but to me it would fit the pattern. So duration of exposure still is a factor in all this, but not a primary one since a lot of psychedelics last for more than an hour.


Experience seems to tell us that beyond very short exposure there is a sort of minimum of a tolerance period. Perhaps weak psychedelics cause no more than a half week's tolerance but less than that is difficult. Perhaps the reason for this minimum is the same reason that the only compounds we include here follow a minimum of affinity and activity so of course the activity you experienced is correlated with the tolerance you get. Coarsely you can say that if you get a super weak trip you have less reason to worry about tolerance than if you get a very strong one.


Comments would be welcome. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

There are a million things I could be wrong about here.

<!-- POST END: id=9848881 -->

As to the debate over tolerance, in my experience it does seem to last much longer than with other, shorter-acting psychedelics. Personally, I have never dosed on occasions that were close enough together to know for sure (after days and days of continuous tripping I'm usually set for awhile.) However, I have dosed from an extremely potent batch with a friend who then took twice the amount we had taken (meaning upwards of 10mg) about 2 weeks later. He hardly tripped at all, and with 10mg of DOC....that's not just a fluke...

<!-- POST START: id=9870576 num=890 author=dustin11928 author_id=158615 date=2011-08-14T06:51:40+0100 -->
### Post #890

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9870576 |
| Author | dustin11928 |
| Author ID | 158615 |
| Date | Aug 14, 2011 at 6:51 AM |
| Page | 45 |

In the last three months I have been experimenting with large doses of DOC, which I have taken orally in diluted water over twenty times at several different doses. At higher doses, +5 mg DOC seems to take you to a more uncontrollable interaction with past memory and therapeutically self reflection somewhat like LSD. I remember at this stage, your mind slips away as I would believe that I had completely died and been introduced to a complete dreamlike reality where usually many negative self realizations were faced and enforced on everything I thought was possible about myself.


I have also found a common bad trip or very powerful trip can be experienced in a spiral of realities where identity lost is common, where you continuously loop in your memories like a movie that continues to fast forward and rewind, I called this the loop. Which was experienced by myself about five times, and seem to activate when there was a lot going on at the location, like loud noise and new people coming into the picture. 


Even at lower doses with inexperienced psychedelic users the loop was common if they were in a uncontrollable environment, it's just their actions and the hallucinations wouldn't be as near as strong as a higher dose. A lot of time for the people who went in the loop, they won't really remember what exactly had happened in till days, weeks, or even months after the comedown. 


After about ten times however with DOC, I had learned what to expect and even if I tried extreme high doses 10mg + I could control it where I wouldn't go in the loop but just have very intense euphoria, mental and physical stimulation, and Beautiful geometric patterns with opened and closed eyes. When the eyes were closed, tunnels of colors would appear, and sometimes mask of entities with past experiences of LSD, DOC, DMT, and psilocybin mushrooms would be seen.


Though there are many profound things I would like to share that this very magical compound has to offer, there is one thing that DOC has shown me that is only comparable to one other substance I have ever done, and that was DMT. With DMT the hallucinations are much more realistic, and much more alive and intense. I had experienced a series of alien abductions with DMT, and those experiences had stayed with me forever. With DOC once however, I did with two other people. I was given 5 drops of DOC diluted into water which was approximately 7 to 8 mg of DOC, my friend was given two which was up to 2 to 5 mg of DOC, and my Uncle was give 8 drops which could of been up to 12mg of DOC. That night turned into a total nightmare as I felt the same alien presence DMT had given me before, I felt as if we all three had been totally abducted by the same force and were experimented with. I had felt is if I were placed in others life, and my deepest secrets had been revealed to everyone in the external world around me, I also felt strange telepathic connections from and external force just like I did on DMT. When I finally started to realize where I was and who I was, I realized I was in the garage walking around after the last thing I remember was being in the car listening to music with my friend and uncle. I look down to see my friend rolling around on the ground completely tranced out, and my uncle still in the car just sitting there, him too tranced out. We all ended up going inside, complete confused at each other, my Uncle was angry for some reason threatening me and my friend. My friend hit the loop after we went inside and was completely spun, and I had finally came down to the DOC high I had been used too, still tripping hard, but nothing like the shit I had just experienced. After the complete come down, my uncle went into a DOC/sleep stage for the next two days while my friend came completely down the following day along with me. None of talked about exactly what had happened in till about a month later when we all felt that a force had placed us in each others lives and we all felt telepathic signals coming towards us from some very strange force. I also will be the first one to tell you that this experience was different than all the others because it wasn't just like I was tripping, it was all so real. It's the things like this that really makes you wonder I suppose.


Also the DOC is active as low as 1mg with threshold effects such as a speedy and low euphoric high with visual distortion. 2-5mg takes up to 2 hours for full affects, however 7-10mg can sometimes be felt within 5 minutes and last up to 20 hours. Usually after 12 hours the affects began to come down and within hours and sleep are completely gone. When snorted the fffects were shorter but kicked in faster. It really stings also, and yes DOC is very bitter.

<!-- POST END: id=9870576 -->

Ah doing the double post thing, but I have some questions about the lovely DOC. 


Have there been many reports of nausea during the come-up? 4-AcO-DMT makes me very nauseous during the comeup if I drink it too fast, and I don't want something similar happening with this. Being nauseous while starting to trip really sucks. 


What sort of relationship does DOC have with marijuana? Will I have any desire to smoke at all? If I do smoke, will it potentiate the DOC? On other psychs, weed has increased the intensity of the visuals for me when I smoke before & during the trip. 


If I take a few mgs to start, how would additional doses work, if at all?

### Post #909

As far as nasea was considered, first two times, I hugged the toilet for a couple seconds. Wasn't bad at all comparably to other phens. Just a quick sick feeling followed by a purge then over. Worst part was maybe feeling continuing nausea for maybe 10 mins. Theres many OTC things people take and claim to work well(ginger. peppermint, dimehydriante(sp)).  I can't remember if nausea is commonly reported with this or not. As for smoking on it. It depends on the person. If you like smoking on other psyches and enjoy the enhancement you'll most likely enjoy it on DOC. The CEV's alone would make me want to tell you to smoke it up atleast once during!

<!-- POST START: id=9893012 num=917 author=PhyllipThylamine author_id=182056 date=2011-08-24T08:14:51+0100 -->
### Post #917

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9893012 |
| Author | PhyllipThylamine |
| Author ID | 182056 |
| Date | Aug 24, 2011 at 8:14 AM |
| Page | 46 |

I recently had my 6th DOC trip! But I still havent gotten above the 1.8mg mark. I'm thoroughly enjoying this compound. There's sometime a little mild nausea on come-up but nothing serious. I usually day-trip coz this stuff is so long-lasting, so usually have perhaps some toast & a coffee in my stomach. If you have any nausea/diahorea issues with this compound I recomend taking it only on an empty stomach. It's perfectly possible to eat on it, once the effects have establised.


I've taken DOC at a London rock fest, using 1.4mg on the Sat & 1mg on the Sunday. These doses are perfectly managable in public & on the tube. The sky looks AWSOME on this psychedelic. I compare DOC to the mushroom experience, except of course it's considerably longer.


On a couple of occassions I've found myself restless-legging in bed, after my gf has gone to sleep & have had to knock it on the head. So far, I've found 20mg of valium or 3 Etizolam is enough, at the tail end of the trip, to kill it & put me to sleep.


DOC has a strong physical push so I excercise heavilly on it, usually in my local park/forest. I'm usually pretty knakkered after a trip but put this down to the walking & incessant laughing. DOC does not appear to have any obvious come-down, though this may be down to my light usage.


I'm now considering adding a shroom-like tryptamine at the DOC peak, as an experiment. Anyone mixed trypts with DOC yet???

<!-- POST END: id=9893012 -->

ok guys im looking for some suggestions on where someone who found 2mgs pretty boring would go next? i had closed eye visuals for a while, had a sort of interesting (very minor and short lived) headspace for a little while, i think i passed out like 8 hours after i took it and i feel pretty much sober now, 10 hours later- id guess i would still have a couple hours to go but i just decided to call it quits with a valium. 


Its definitely something id like to explore more but i found this dose wholly uninteresting, sort of had to entertain myself for a while and then finally just decided to look at minor closed eye visuals for a while. I really thought the headspace was pretty mild and calm too, which makes me think i could probably handle myself on a little bit bigger of a dose. anyway if anyone has any suggestions for where i should jump to next- or where someone with a similar experience to mine found they enjoyed it a lot more.


fyi- i usually dont get a very strong effect from ampetamines- (natural tolerance?)  mdma tolerance could be an issue, and i did dose mescaline -(also to very minor effects) two weeks ago. oh also this is the european batch not the purple one.

i'd be hesitant to increase dosage by more than 1-1.2mg's just because the dosage response curb is quite steep for most individuals.  Also a good idea to wait at least 2 weeks between experiences to avoid tolerance. ~2.55mg of the european batch was a strong +++ for me, but YMMV of course.

> Click to expand...
> — Swedish Penguin said:


If it's tolerance you just need to leave it a bit. If you're a big lad who takes alot of phens & phets, I can imagine a kinda "double-cross-tolerance" what with Doc having both psychedelic & stimulant effects.


If you insist on trying again without a *completely* clean break, from ALL psychoactives, I wouldnt bump up by more than a milligram. So perhaps 3mg... try that. If that doesnt do it for you it may be that you have some natural immunity to something in this compound. Don't get too confident though, or it might bite you in the ass!


Best of luck!

Best of luck ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

### Post #926

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|

How are folks with doing this in a big crowd?  There's a HUUUUGE fireworks show this Sunday near me, draws 500,000 to the Ohio River in front of Cincinnati (the very intense, highly venerated WEBN "Riverfest" show).  I have gone to it almost every time last 30 years, and I have a very good well practiced plan I used the last 6 or 7 times to beat MOST of the gridlock afterwards... I park at a location that is about a 45min walk from the show, that is right by the freeway, and walk up there... it's a little tiring but not much.  Get to a spot behind people on the floodwall who had been camping out there all day, put on my headphones tuned to the station for the soundtrack and wait about an hour, which is the most tedious part.  Then when its done, hightail it back to the car.  Just me on my own, so there's no one to loose or keep track of.  I know the area so well I could do the walk with my eyes closed, and the whole thing is VERY familiar to me, so anxiety should not be an issue.


ANYWAY I have not tried the DOC yet (but am VERY experienced in all sorts of psychedelics and RCs) and am thinking of trying a first-time dose of 2mg, of the purple batch for this  From what I've read that SHOULD be in the moderate range of strength.


I know it tends to be speedy and so I am thinking that it should make the walk a breeze.  But I am wondering how others have felt exerting themselves like this on DOC, and also standing around waiting in an enormous crowd but I will be at the BACK of 99.999% of them in my vicinity, so I won't be crowded in or smooshed in any way at all... behind me might be a couple people then a downsloping hill in the direction back to the car with mostly empty space when the show is over, though it quickly fills with people leaving.


Does the speedy energy tend to keep you feeling "UP" and in a positive headspace?  Or is there any likelihood of getting dizzy or fatigued or upset about the crowd?  I've done this event on shrooms (which were frankly a bit much in this throng but I handled it fine), LSD (fine & excellent), 2C-I (about perfect actually, with its speediness and anti-headfuck clear-mind tendencies).  But I was hoping for something a bit more visual than 2C-I which only tends to enhance colors and give trails, so was thinking DOC might be more perfect.  The dose is really the only issue, and the fact that it will be my 1st time doing it.


Any thoughts about this plan or stories from others who have done anything remotely similar while on a modest hit of DOC greatly appreciated.

<!-- POST END: id=9909511 -->

I'm not usually a social tripper atleast in big groups but IMO DOC would be one of the ones I wouldn't mind doing in a large setting. Its pretty calm even when its say agitating during the come up or something. I also find walking on DOC to be easy, probably because of the stimulation and actually mostly find myself doing things like, chopping firewood, cleaning, or pretty much anything that involves somewhat full body movement during the come up. 3 hours in is when I would take a break and start relaxing. As far as dosing, you might as well do it a few hours early since like you stated this one has atleast a 12 hour duration for everyone and never lasts under 20 hours for me personally, like you said you will be able to become comfortable in your trip. 


Besides that I plan on trying 2c-P+DOC in around a month or so. Have to venture back a little into the P realm first.

<!-- POST START: id=9910679 num=933 author=clubberdude author_id=184317 date=2011-09-01T16:57:04+0100 -->
### Post #933

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9910679 |
| Author | clubberdude |
| Author ID | 184317 |
| Date | Sep 1, 2011 at 4:57 PM |
| Page | 47 |

Might be giving this little baby another ride tomorrow night - at a relatively low dose (3-4 mg max), though may insuffliate it exclusively, as I a) want a relatively short trip, and b) want to build a cross-section of its effects via this ROA. Of course, much depends on how many things I manage to get done tomorrow - have quite a few things to sort out.


To the poster above, the only way you'll be able to characterise its effects using that ROA is to try it yourself. Very few people (relatively speaking) have taken DOC, even fewer have smoked it. Hell I may even try this myself one day. All I will say, especially given the lack of data on safety, is start low (1-2 mg maximum), and leave it a while before redosing. I would have absolutely no idea how the bioavailability parameters differ according to the differing ROA's, and I'm not sure that data exists online (I'll probably have a little look later on).

<!-- POST END: id=9910679 -->

> [DwayneHoover said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9909511)
> 
> 
> 
> 			How are folks with doing this in a big crowd?  There's a HUUUUGE fireworks show this Sunday near me, draws 500,000 to the Ohio River in front of Cincinnati (the very intense, highly venerated WEBN "Riverfest" show).  I have gone to it almost every time last 30 years, and I have a very good well practiced plan I used the last 6 or 7 times to beat MOST of the gridlock afterwards... I park at a location that is about a 45min walk from the show, that is right by the freeway, and walk up there... it's a little tiring but not much.  Get to a spot behind people on the floodwall who had been camping out there all day, put on my headphones tuned to the station for the soundtrack and wait about an hour, which is the most tedious part.  Then when its done, hightail it back to the car.  Just me on my own, so there's no one to loose or keep track of.  I know the area so well I could do the walk with my eyes closed, and the whole thing is VERY familiar to me, so anxiety should not be an issue.
> 
> 
> 
> ANYWAY I have not tried the DOC yet (but am VERY experienced in all sorts of psychedelics and RCs) and am thinking of trying a first-time dose of 2mg, of the purple batch for this  From what I've read that SHOULD be in the moderate range of strength.
> 
> 
> 
> I know it tends to be speedy and so I am thinking that it should make the walk a breeze.  But I am wondering how others have felt exerting themselves like this on DOC, and also standing around waiting in an enormous crowd but I will be at the BACK of 99.999% of them in my vicinity, so I won't be crowded in or smooshed in any way at all... behind me might be a couple people then a downsloping hill in the direction back to the car with mostly empty space when the show is over, though it quickly fills with people leaving.
> 
> 
> 
> Does the speedy energy tend to keep you feeling "UP" and in a positive headspace?  Or is there any likelihood of getting dizzy or fatigued or upset about the crowd?  I've done this event on shrooms (which were frankly a bit much in this throng but I handled it fine), LSD (fine & excellent), 2C-I (about perfect actually, with its speediness and anti-headfuck clear-mind tendencies).  But I was hoping for something a bit more visual than 2C-I which only tends to enhance colors and give trails, so was thinking DOC might be more perfect.  The dose is really the only issue, and the fact that it will be my 1st time doing it.
> 
> 
> 
> Any thoughts about this plan or stories from others who have done anything remotely similar while on a modest hit of DOC greatly appreciated.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — DwayneHoover said:


Sounds fun!  The only thing i would be concerned about is driving. DOC, for me, was very intensely visual & totally fucked my depth perception.  Driving was definitely not a possibility until about T+21.  Although things died down substantially after about T+14, i then slept for about 7hrs, & woke up still of baseline, but mostly functional.  If you have a ride, i'd say go for it.  I could interact with people perfectly fine on 2.55mg, perhaps even a bit more outgoing than normal.  I also experienced some of the most intense visuals i've had in quite a long time.  Walls totally melting & such, CEV's of surreal vistas etc, good times.  Head felt pretty clear the whole time though.  And in regards to dosage timing, i'd probably dose 5-6hrs before the fireworks show just so i was well acclimated to the trip before venturing out.  Also that gives you the option of deciding not to go out if you don't feel it would be a good idea (i'd bet the possibility of that would be pretty low.)  


I didn't really find it stimulating in the traditional sense of the word.  Not at all like 2c-i's stimulation.  I definitely wasn't going to sleep during the thick of things, not so much because i was stimulated physically, things were just too damn interesting to entertain the thought of sleep, lol.  Overall, i was quite relaxed, laying on my couch just listening to music & watching the walls melt, spin, twirl, etc, for a large portion of the experience, no desire to pace around the apartment or go for a light jog like i get with some psychedelics.  Though as always, YMMV ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

According to a friend who recently supplied me with a couple very small batches of DOC his other DOxx compounds have lasted indefinitely when diluted in regular vodka & stored in the cold & dark. 


I am (perhaps unnecessarilly) wary about the other DOxx compounds but I think the world of DOC & cannot recomend it enough. It is strong, long stuff & should be used only by those with good physical & mental fortitude.


For the Cinncinati fire-works man, I do seriously hope you did not & do not intend to drive whilst intoxicated even slightly on a psychedelic. This is irresponsible in the extreme. Whatever you do that brings risk to your own life & limb you are completely free to do without limitation. As soon as your actions bring risk to the life & limb of others, you're dangerously negligent. Don't do it! If you're an experienced tripper, I really should not have to say this!

### Post #957

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9958358 |
| Author | reformer |
| Author ID | 167135 |
| Date | Sep 22, 2011 at 7:03 AM |
| Page | 48 |

**Selecting Cl^3: Amount, ROA and Timing**


Intrigued by these relative PKs and effects, how would one go about designing a timeline for researching the three prototypes/generations of 4-position Cl-derivatized phenethylamines?


Looking for tips on interactions of DOC with 2C-C and 25C-NBOMe, and how to set up an initial, conservative combination including timeline & ROA.


Thinking something like:


t+0:00 = 1.5 mg DOC via dissolved liquid insufflation (LI) [aiming for reduced length of effect and increased early onset with this ROA]

t+2:00 = 20 mg 2C-C via oral

t+4:00 = 0.7 mg 25C-NBOMe via buccal blotter


With the idea to build in intensity throughout, and have a common decline so that at ~t+9:00-10:00 the effects are largely disappearing. 


Tried these individually already, but not not DOC via LI. The real questions here revolve around: 1) Amount; 2) ROA; 3) Timing.


A modeling way to do this would be to bracket the conservative outlier conditions and to perform the minimal number of experiences needed to determine what condition provides best results (although environment (set and setting) are going to make it difficult to draw strict conclusions).


But who has time to try [ROA X multiple amounts X multiple RC] combos?... While including appropriate tolerance breaks in between trials.


Any tips on negative interactions, timing, amounts in combination and ROAs are appreciated!

<!-- POST END: id=9958358 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=9958957 num=958 author=clubberdude author_id=184317 date=2011-09-22T15:44:40+0100 -->
### Post #958

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9958957 |
| Author | clubberdude |
| Author ID | 184317 |
| Date | Sep 22, 2011 at 3:44 PM |
| Page | 48 |

Insufflation of DOC doesn't appear to significantly reduce the overall duration of the chemical, (say 18-22 hours maybe as opposed to 24 hours dosing orally). Be very aware that come up on insufflated DOC is almost instantaneous - I was feeling altered within 15-20 seconds, and beginning to fully trip within 3-4 minutes! ![8o](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/eek.gif)

<!-- POST END: id=9958957 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9959613 num=960 author=Addam author_id=163277 date=2011-09-22T21:28:12+0100 -->
### Post #960

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9959613 |
| Author | Addam |
| Author ID | 163277 |
| Date | Sep 22, 2011 at 9:28 PM |
| Page | 48 |

OOoooo, a Chloro triple stack! Very interesting. My instincts tell me this would be a lovely experience. I have no experience with a similar combo, or even with all the substances being discussed, so my contribution here is merely conjecture.


I might bump the time of 2C-C up to +1:30 instead of +2:00 (that is if we're trying to coincide a peak).  2C-C usually takes an hour to begin effect, for me anyways.

I might also hasten the administration of the 25C. I have no experience with 25C yet, but from my understanding it's around 1-1:30 for peak with buccal? So, if I were doing this and intended to have some coinciding peaks, I'd administer the 25C at t+3:00. 5 hour duration would start bringing you down around the ~9:00 mark, around the time the DOC would likely be waning as well (depending on your individual metabolism of course).


There's scattered reports of vasoconstriction with 25C, but not prevalent, seems dependent on the individual. So that and DOC's possible vasoconstriction (again, doesn't seem to be ALL individuals) might make that something to watch for. Not saying it's a certainty by any means, but keep your eyes open for that. I've heard of people supplementing a few grams of L-Arginine to combat this, which helps the production of Nitric Oxide, a vasodilator, as I'm sure you're well aware.

That's the only obvious potential negative interaction that I can see. Anyone else with more 25C experience should speak up though.

I wish you a safe journey, and be sure to tell us about it :D

<!-- POST END: id=9959613 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9963518 num=965 author=jamaica0535 author_id=96351 date=2011-09-24T12:07:41+0100 -->
### Post #965

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9963518 |
| Author | jamaica0535 |
| Author ID | 96351 |
| Date | Sep 24, 2011 at 12:07 PM |
| Page | 49 |

The whole thing was a really unpleasant experience and it happened some time ago, but I will try to go more into it. 


Basically we let someone measure out 2 doses of DOB, and he gave us both way more than we had any desire to take that evening. 


First alerts included nausea sometime after an hour into the 2nd.


The 18 hour peak that gave way from that was spent locked in an apartment trying to maintain some form of sanity. Very shakey, overly stimulating in the way that a failed suicide attempt with a bottle of ritalin would be overly stimulating. We weren't quite at a level that we felt worried about our health as much as our sanity. It was so intense that we were not functional enough to operate a coloring book and crayon for 8 hours of it. After we mastered the crayon, we moved to permanent marker and a friend's tent for a canvas. She was pissed about it later, but it was not directed at me despite it being half my fault. 


Lots of crazy stuff drawn in tent. It has become daylight again, I step outside to a cold day. Its winter, but the landscape at +18h appears to be more along the lines of Saharan desert from the way its moving. Still going way too hard for normal society.


I attempted origami, found myself too shakey and gave up. Tried to amuse ourselves, smoked a lot of weed in the 8 hours that followed.  Long 8 hours of coming down, folded some paper cranes and glued them to a dead bonsai tree. Sleep didn't come for around +36h from initial dose.


The entire experience was really unpleasant, like the sort of unpleasant that makes stabbing myself in the hand more appealing than another DOB overdose.

<!-- POST END: id=9963518 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9968107 num=967 author=JBrandon author_id=138901 date=2011-09-26T17:22:32+0100 -->
### Post #967

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9968107 |
| Author | JBrandon |
| Author ID | 138901 |
| Date | Sep 26, 2011 at 5:22 PM |
| Page | 49 |

Yes, haldol, quietiapine, or risperidone. You should also have some kind of benzo available.


Make sure you have one of those three anti-psychotics (I recommend the risperidone highly) before you get heavy into the long acting psychs. You will be so glad you did when the time comes to stop a terrible trip at hour 6 vs riding it out for 2 days.

<!-- POST END: id=9968107 -->

Plus, since I was already coming up when it happened, it wasn't awful, unlike puking from alcohol.


Oh, and I definitely say this was a ++++ trip, although at times it receded to a +++. Holy shit, I can't wait to do it again in the future at this dose. Or maybe a little higher?

I had pretty much left the psychedelics this time 2 years ago, I'd found my niche with MDMA & I was more than happy. Shrooms would be eaten on the odd occassion I had the opportunity but I wasnt into experimenting anymore...


Then the government banned Meph. I tried the stuff out, liked it (bit too much) & began searching for LSD like chemicals (2c's, tryptamines etc) & have been enjoying tripping regularly for about a year now.

DOC is by far the most facinating chemical & I am delighted to have discovered it!


I dunno much about aMT, but I believe it is in fact DOC that's the cadillac of psychedelics!

aMT and DOC... One can only wonder what this combination would be like... I'd imagine the full range of virtually anything could be experienced on this combination. Feels like it could be near the ultimate psychedelic experience.


Well in the interest of science and all that, and the mere fundamental paradigm of curiosity killing cats, and envelope pushing, I think this may well have to be tested soon... Maybe with a bit of Ketamine thrown in if I'm feeling brave enough (or stupid perhaps...)... Crazy times for sure! Has anyone else combined these two (+ possibly third...) lovely chemicals? Did it end badly? Was it as promising as my imagination thinks it might be? 


I'd be separating the peaks slightly (by say 3-4 hours just in-case of MAOI effects), and going fairly careful on the doses of each. Something tells me this will be intense. Boredom and Intrigue - a dangerous mix...


I'd say DOC more resembles a maglev-train, going through the Himalayas - smooth, but at the same time, completely batshit-insane!

Another lovely DOC trip yesterday. The come down is a real bitch though. Couldn't sleep until at least 20 hours in, and then I only slept on and off for a few hours. But, the experience itself makes it all worth it. I can't believe the visuals that I have been getting with this compound. Unfortunately, my trip mates don't see the visuals in nearly the intensity that I have. I wonder why this is.

> Click to expand...
> — Axed said:


Visualization isn't exclusive to psychedelic experience. I truly believe some are just more prone to these effects than others, I have friends who get nearly zero visual disturbances at all from LSD. 2C-B has made this lesson all the more clear to me; psychedelic visuals are as much an effect of the drug as they are an exercise of your own mind. I can manipulate my 2C-B visuals as much as I want to.. You probably just engage yourself in the visuals more than your friends.

<!-- POST END: id=10090273 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10102411 num=1 author=clubberdude author_id=184317 date=2011-11-18T00:58:48+0000 -->
### Post #1

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 10102411 |
| Author | clubberdude |
| Author ID | 184317 |
| Date | Nov 18, 2011 at 12:58 AM |
| Page | 51 |

Oh weeks ago now, probably approaching 2 months ago now. I doubt tolerance was an issue.


I find DOC has a hideous comedown, on a par with high, repeated dosed MDMA. This doesn't seem unreasonable given that the euphoria from it equals peak level of what I might obtain from an optimal dose of MDMA, its just (generally) trippy-as-fuck to go with it. The next few days though, wow! A very worthy chemical but the comedown is a bitch! Be prepared for that! Still want more though, I guess the workaround here is to avoid concomittant use of putative 5HT agonists in conjunction with DOC.

<!-- POST END: id=10102411 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10103653 num=1 author=Axed author_id=179566 date=2011-11-18T14:50:28+0000 -->

| Post ID | 10103653 |

The comedown is really shitty. As I wind down the trip, I find myself really sore (especially my back/shoulders/neck area) and exhausted, but of course still stimmed up for a while. And then for the next few days, I can't seem to get good sleep, and my legs feel weird and sore. But it's worth it every now and then for an awesome DOC trip.

<!-- POST END: id=10103653 -->

I don't experience any negative effects during the comedown from DOC, rather the opposite actually. The afterglow from a DOC experience is one of the best. However, I agree that the euphoric empathy during the DOC experience is amazing, and actually - in my experience - blows the euphoria from MDMA out of the water.


> [Axed said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=10090004)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Another lovely DOC trip yesterday. The come down is a real bitch though. Couldn't sleep until at least 20 hours in, and then I only slept on and off for a few hours. But, the experience itself makes it all worth it. I can't believe the visuals that I have been getting with this compound. Unfortunately, my trip mates don't see the visuals in nearly the intensity that I have. I wonder why this is.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Axed said:


It usually takes me about 24 hours to sleep after dosing DOC. I have used diazepam once to get to sleep after being kept awake by hypnic jerks even at 24 hours. It's more a case that your body is so relaxed and ready for sleep, but your mind is still pumping. Still, it's not an agressive insomnia and I find the sleep following a DOC session to be so deep and refreshing.


The visuals are immense indeed, the CEVs take me to another world. They are also incredibly meaningful in a very cosmic way. Highly colourful, spectacular resolution and detail. The fractals go on forever. I can get lost in the mental/visual landscape for hours on DOC, it is that absorbing.

<!-- POST END: id=10104645 -->
